<p data-tool="mdnice编辑器" style="color: rgb(74, 74, 74); font-size: 16px; line-height: 1.8em; letter-spacing: 0.02em; text-align: left; text-indent: 0em; margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; padding-top: 20px; padding-bottom: 8px; padding-left: 0px; padding-right: 0px;"><strong style="color: rgb(0, 0, 0); font-weight: bold; background-attachment: scroll; background-clip: border-box; background-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0); background-image: none; background-origin: padding-box; background-position-x: left; background-position-y: top; background-repeat: no-repeat; background-size: auto; width: auto; height: auto; margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; padding-top: 0px; padding-bottom: 0px; padding-left: 0px; padding-right: 0px; border-top-style: none; border-bottom-style: none; border-left-style: none; border-right-style: none; border-top-width: 3px; border-bottom-width: 3px; border-left-width: 3px; border-right-width: 3px; border-top-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.4); border-bottom-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.4); border-left-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.4); border-right-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.4); border-top-left-radius: 0px; border-top-right-radius: 0px; border-bottom-right-radius: 0px; border-bottom-left-radius: 0px;">"情况明、决心大、方法对"这九个字，并不在《毛选》的某一篇文章里，而是毛泽东在1961年1月的一次中央工作会议上说的。</strong></p>
<p data-tool="mdnice编辑器" style="color: rgb(74, 74, 74); font-size: 16px; line-height: 1.8em; letter-spacing: 0.02em; text-align: left; text-indent: 0em; margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; padding-top: 20px; padding-bottom: 8px; padding-left: 0px; padding-right: 0px;">背景：</p>
<ul data-tool="mdnice编辑器" style="list-style-type: disc; margin-top: 8px; margin-bottom: 8px; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; padding-top: 0px; padding-bottom: 0px; padding-left: 25px; padding-right: 0px; color: rgb(0, 0, 0);">

border-top-left-radius: 0px; border-top-right-radius: 0px; border-bottom-right-radius: 0px; border-bottom-left-radius: 0px;">时间</strong>：1961年1月</section></li><li><section style="margin-top: 5px; margin-bottom: 5px; color: rgb(1, 1, 1); font-size: 16px; line-height: 1.8em; letter-spacing: 0em; text-align: left; font-weight: normal;"><strong style="color: rgb(0, 0, 0); font-weight: bold; background-attachment: scroll; <p style="text-indent: 0em; padding-top: 20px; padding-bottom: 8px; padding-left: 0px; padding-right: 0px; color: rgb(89, 89, 89); font-size: 16px; line-height: 1.8em; letter-spacing: 0em; text-align: left; font-weight: normal; margin-top: 0px; margin-right: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; margin-left: 0px;">"今后工作中要做到三条：情况明，决心大，方法对。"</p>
</blockquote>
</section></li></ul>
<p data-tool="mdnice编辑器" style="color: rgb(74, 74, 74); font-size: 16px; line-height: 1.8em; letter-spacing: 0.02em; text-align: left; text-indent: 0em; margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; padding-top: 20px; padding-bottom: 8px; padding-left: 0px; padding-right: 0px;">这句话后来被收录在：</p>
<ul data-tool="mdnice编辑器" style="list-style-type: disc; margin-top: 8px; margin-bottom: 8px; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; padding-top: 0px; padding-bottom: 0px; padding-left: 25px; padding-right: 0px; color: rgb(0, 0, 0);">
<li><section style="margin-top: 5px; margin-bottom: 5px; color: rgb(1, 1, 1); font-size: 16px; line-height: 1.8em; letter-spacing: 0em; text-align: left; font-weight: normal;">《毛泽东文集》第八卷</section></li><li><section style="margin-top: 5px; margin-bottom: 5px; color: rgb(1, 1, 1); font-size: 16px; line-height: 1.8em; letter-spacing: 0em; text-align: left; font-weight: normal;">《建国以来毛泽东文稿》第九册</section></li></ul>
<p data-tool="mdnice编辑器" style="color: rgb(74, 74, 74); font-size: 16px; line-height: 1.8em; letter-spacing: 0.02em; text-align: left; text-indent: 0em; margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; padding-top: 20px; padding-bottom: 8px; padding-left: 0px; padding-right: 0px;"><strong style="color: rgb(0, 0, 0); font-weight: bold; background-attachment: scroll; background-clip: border-box; background-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0); background-image: none; background-origin: padding-box; background-position-x: left; background-position-y: top; background-repeat: no-repeat; background-size: auto; width: auto; height: auto; margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; padding-top: 0px; padding-bottom: 0px; padding-left: 0px; padding-right: 0px; border-top-style: none; border-bottom-style: none; border-left-style: none; border-right-style: none; border-top-width: 3px; border-bottom-width: 3px; border-left-width: 3px; border-right-width: 3px; border-top-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.4); border-bottom-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.4); border-left-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.4); border-right-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.4); border-top-left-radius: 0px; border-top-right-radius: 0px; border-bottom-right-radius: 0px; border-bottom-left-radius: 0px;">但是</strong>，虽然这九个字是在1961年才明确提出的，这套思想却贯穿了《毛选》的始终。</p>
<hr data-tool="mdnice编辑器" style="margin-top: 10px; margin-bottom: 10px; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; padding-top: 0px; padding-bottom: 0px; padding-left: 0px; padding-right: 0px; border-top-style: none; border-bottom-style: none; border-left-style: none; border-right-style: none; border-top-width: 1px; border-bottom-width: 3px; border-left-width: 3px; border-right-width: 3px; border-top-color: rgb(0, 0, 0); border-bottom-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.4); border-left-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.4); border-right-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.4); border-top-left-radius: 0px; border-top-right-radius: 0px; border-bottom-right-radius: 0px; border-bottom-left-radius: 0px; background-attachment: scroll; background-clip: border-box; background-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0); background-image: linear-gradient(90deg, rgba(60, 112, 198, 0) 0%, rgba(60, 122, 198, 0.75) 50%, rgba(60, 122, 198, 0) 100%); background-origin: padding-box; background-position-x: left; background-position-y: top; background-repeat: no-repeat; background-size: auto; width: auto; height: 1px;">
<h2 data-tool="mdnice编辑器" style="margin-top: 30px; margin-bottom: 15px; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; padding-left: 0px; padding-right: 0px; border-top-style: none; background-attachment: scroll; background-clip: border-box; background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255); background-image: url('https://files.mdnice.com/mountain_2.png'); background-origin: padding-box; background-position-x: center; background-position-y: center; background-repeat: no-repeat; background-size: 63px; width: auto; height: auto; align-items: unset; border-bottom-style: none; border-left-style: none; border-right-style: none; border-top-width: 1px; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-left-width: 1px; border-right-width: 1px; border-top-color: rgb(0, 0, 0); border-bottom-color: rgb(0, 0, 0); border-left-color: rgb(0, 0, 0); border-right-color: rgb(0, 0, 0); border-top-left-radius: 0px; border-top-right-radius: 0px; border-bottom-left-radius: 0px; border-bottom-right-radius: 0px; box-shadow: none; display: flex; flex-direction: unset; float: unset; justify-content: center; line-height: 1.5em; overflow-x: unset; overflow-y: unset; padding-top: 0px; padding-bottom: 0px; position: relative; text-align: left; text-shadow: none; transform: none; -webkit-box-reflect: unset;"><span class="prefix" style="display: none;"></span><span class="content" style="font-size: 18px; color: rgb(60, 112, 198); line-height: 2.4em; letter-spacing: 0em; margin-top: 38px; margin-bottom: 10px; border-bottom-style: none; border-left-style: none; border-right-style: none; border-top-width: 1px; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-left-width: 1px; border-right-width: 1px; border-top-color: rgb(0, 0, 0); border-bottom-color: rgb(0, 0, 0); border-left-color: rgb(0, 0, 0); border-right-color: rgb(0, 0, 0); border-top-left-radius: 0px; border-top-right-radius: 0px; border-bottom-left-radius: 0px; border-bottom-right-radius: 0px; align-items: unset; background-attachment: scroll; background-clip: border-box; background-color: transparent; background-image: none; background-origin: padding-box; background-position-x: 0%; background-position-y: 0%; background-repeat: no-repeat; background-size: auto; border-top-style: none; box-shadow: none; display: inline-block; font-weight: bold; flex-direction: unset; float: unset; height: 38px; justify-content: unset; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; overflow-x: unset; overflow-y: unset; padding-top: 0px; padding-bottom: 0px; padding-left: 0px; padding-right: 0px; position: relative; text-align: center; text-indent: 0em; text-shadow: none; transform: none; width: auto; -webkit-box-reflect: unset;">二、这套思想在《毛选》里的核心文章</span><span class="suffix" style="display: none;"></span></h2>
<p data-tool="mdnice编辑器" style="color: rgb(74, 74, 74); font-size: 16px; line-height: 1.8em; letter-spacing: 0.02em; text-align: left; text-indent: 0em; margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; padding-top: 20px; padding-bottom: 8px; padding-left: 0px; padding-right: 0px;"><strong style="color: rgb(0, 0, 0); font-weight: bold; background-attachment: scroll; background-clip: border-box; background-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0); background-image: none; background-origin: padding-box; background-position-x: left; background-position-y: top; background-repeat: no-repeat; background-size: auto; width: auto; height: auto; margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; padding-top: 0px; padding-bottom: 0px; padding-left: 0px; padding-right: 0px; border-top-style: none; border-bottom-style: none; border-left-style: none; border-right-style: none; border-top-width: 3px; border-bottom-width: 3px; border-left-width: 3px; border-right-width: 3px; border-top-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.4); border-bottom-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.4); border-left-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.4); border-right-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.4); border-top-left-radius: 0px; border-top-right-radius: 0px; border-bottom-right-radius: 0px; border-bottom-left-radius: 0px;">情况明、决心大、方法对</strong>作为一个完整表述出现得晚，但它的思想源头可以追溯到《毛选》的多篇经典文章。：</p>
<h3 data-tool="mdnice编辑器" style="margin-top: 30px; margin-bottom: 15px; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; padding-top: 0px; padding-bottom: 0px; padding-left: 0px; padding-right: 0px; align-items: unset; background-attachment: scroll; background-clip: border-box; background-color: transparent; background-image: none; background-origin: padding-box; background-position-x: 0%; background-position-y: 0%; background-repeat: no-repeat; background-size: auto; border-top-style: none; border-bottom-style: none; border-left-style: none; border-right-style: none; border-top-width: 1px; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-left-width: 1px; border-right-width: 1px; border-top-color: rgb(0, 0, 0); border-bottom-color: rgb(0, 0, 0); border-left-color: rgb(0, 0, 0); border-right-color: rgb(0, 0, 0); border-top-left-radius: 0px; border-top-right-radius: 0px; border-bottom-left-radius: 0px; border-bottom-right-radius: 0px; box-shadow: none; display: block; flex-direction: unset; float: unset; height: auto; justify-content: unset; line-height: 1.5em; overflow-x: unset; overflow-y: unset; position: relative; text-align: left; text-shadow: none; transform: none; width: auto; -webkit-box-reflect: unset;"><span style="background-attachment: scroll; background-clip: border-box; background-color: transparent; background-image: url('https://files.mdnice.com/mountain_1.png'); background-origin: padding-box; background-position-x: 0%; background-position-y: 0%; background-repeat: no-repeat; background-size: 15px 15px; width: 15px; height: 15px; align-items: unset; border-top-style: none; border-bottom-style: none; border-left-style: none; border-right-style: none; border-top-width: 1px; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-left-width: 1px; border-right-width: 1px; border-top-color: rgb(0, 0, 0); border-bottom-color: rgb(0, 0, 0); border-left-color: rgb(0, 0, 0); border-right-color: rgb(0, 0, 0); border-top-left-radius: 0px; border-top-right-radius: 0px; border-bottom-left-radius: 0px; border-bottom-right-radius: 0px; box-shadow: none; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); display: inline-block; font-size: 22px; font-weight: bold; flex-direction: unset; float: unset; justify-content: unset; letter-spacing: 0px; line-height: 1.5em; margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: -2px; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; overflow-x: unset; overflow-y: unset; padding-top: 0px; padding-bottom: 0px; padding-left: 0px; padding-right: 0px; position: relative; text-align: left; text-indent: 0em; text-shadow: none; transform: none; -webkit-box-reflect: unset;"></span><span class="prefix" style="display: none;"></span><span class="content" style="font-size: 16px; color: rgb(60, 112, 198); line-height: 1.5em; letter-spacing: 0em; align-items: unset; background-attachment: scroll; background-clip: border-box; background-color: transparent; background-image: none; background-origin: padding-box; background-position-x: 0%; background-position-y: 0%; background-repeat: no-repeat; background-size: auto; border-top-style: none; border-bottom-style: none; border-left-style: none; border-right-style: none; border-top-width: 1px; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-left-width: 1px; border-right-width: 1px; border-top-color: rgb(0, 0, 0); border-bottom-color: rgb(0, 0, 0); border-left-color: rgb(0, 0, 0); border-right-color: rgb(0, 0, 0); border-top-left-radius: 0px; border-top-right-radius: 0px; border-bottom-left-radius: 0px; border-bottom-right-radius: 0px; box-shadow: none; display: inline-block; font-weight: bold; flex-direction: unset; float: unset; height: auto; justify-content: unset; margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; margin-left: 8px; margin-right: 0px; overflow-x: unset; overflow-y: unset; padding-top: 0px; padding-bottom: 0px; padding-left: 0px; padding-right: 0px; position: relative; text-align: left; text-indent: 0em; text-shadow: none; transform: none; width: auto; -webkit-box-reflect: unset;">1. 【情况明】的思想源头</span><span class="suffix" style="display: none;"></span></h3>
<h4 data-tool="mdnice编辑器" style="margin-top: 30px; margin-bottom: 15px; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; padding-top: 0px; padding-bottom: 0px; padding-left: 0px; padding-right: 0px; display: block;"><span class="prefix" style="display: none;"></span><span class="content" style="font-size: 18px; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 1.5em; letter-spacing: 0em; text-align: left; font-weight: bold; display: block;">最核心的文章：《反对本本主义》（1930年5月）</span><span class="suffix" style="display: none;"></span></h4>
<p data-tool="mdnice编辑器" style="color: rgb(74, 74, 74); font-size: 16px; line-height: 1.8em; letter-spacing: 0.02em; text-align: left; text-indent: 0em; margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; padding-top: 20px; padding-bottom: 8px; padding-left: 0px; padding-right: 0px;"><strong style="color: rgb(0, 0, 0); font-weight: bold; background-attachment: scroll; background-clip: border-box; background-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0); background-image: none; background-origin: padding-box; background-position-x: left; background-position-y: top; background-repeat: no-repeat; background-size: auto; width: auto; height: auto; margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; padding-top: 0px; padding-bottom: 0px; padding-left: 0px; padding-right: 0px; border-top-style: none; border-bottom-style: none; border-left-style: none; border-right-style: none; border-top-width: 3px; border-bottom-width: 3px; border-left-width: 3px; border-right-width: 3px; border-top-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.4); border-bottom-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.4); border-left-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.4); border-right-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.4); border-top-left-radius: 0px; border-top-right-radius: 0px; border-bottom-right-radius: 0px; border-bottom-left-radius: 0px;">原名</strong>：《调查工作》</p>
<p data-tool="mdnice编辑器" style="color: rgb(74, 74, 74); font-size: 16px; line-height: 1.8em; letter-spacing: 0.02em; text-align: left; text-indent: 0em; margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; padding-top: 20px; padding-bottom: 8px; padding-left: 0px; padding-right: 0px;"><strong style="color: rgb(0, 0, 0); font-weight: bold; background-attachment: scroll; background-clip: border-box; background-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0); background-image: none; background-origin: padding-box; background-position-x: left; background-position-y: top; background-repeat: no-repeat; background-size: auto; width: auto; height: auto; margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; padding-top: 0px; padding-bottom: 0px; padding-left: 0px; padding-right: 0px; border-top-style: none; border-bottom-style: none; border-left-style: none; border-right-style: none; border-top-width: 3px; border-bottom-width: 3px; border-left-width: 3px; border-right-width: 3px; border-top-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.4); border-bottom-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.4); border-left-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.4); border-right-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.4); border-top-left-radius: 0px; border-top-right-radius: 0px; border-bottom-right-radius: 0px; border-bottom-left-radius: 0px;">核心金句</strong>：</p>
<blockquote class="custom-blockquote multiquote-1" data-tool="mdnice编辑器" style="margin-top: 20px; margin-bottom: 20px; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; padding-top: 10px; padding-bottom: 10px; padding-left: 20px; padding-right: 10px; border-top-style: none; border-bottom-style: none; border-left-style: none; border-right-style: none; border-top-width: 3px; border-bottom-width: 3px; border-left-width: 3px; border-right-width: 3px; border-top-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.4); border-bottom-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.4); border-left-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.4); border-right-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.4); border-top-left-radius: 0px; border-top-right-radius: 0px; border-bottom-right-radius: 0px; border-bottom-left-radius: 0px; background-attachment: scroll; background-clip: border-box; background-color: rgb(239, 239, 239); background-image: none; background-origin: padding-box; background-position-x: left; background-position-y: top; background-repeat: no-repeat; background-size: auto; width: auto; height: auto; box-shadow: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0) 0px 0px 0px 0px; display: block; overflow-x: auto; overflow-y: auto;"><span style="display: none; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); font-size: 16px; line-height: 1.5em; letter-spacing: 0em; text-align: left; font-weight: normal;"></span>
<p style="text-indent: 0em; padding-top: 20px; padding-bottom: 8px; padding-left: 0px; padding-right: 0px; color: rgb(89, 89, 89); font-size: 16px; line-height: 1.8em; letter-spacing: 0em; text-align: left; font-weight: normal; margin-top: 0px; margin-right: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; margin-left: 0px;">"没有调查，没有发言权。"<br>
"你对于那个问题不能解决吗？那你就去调查那个问题的现状和它的历史吧！你完完全全调查明白了，你对那个问题就有解决的办法了。"</p>
</blockquote>
<p data-tool="mdnice编辑器" style="color: rgb(74, 74, 74); font-size: 16px; line-height: 1.8em; letter-spacing: 0.02em; text-align: left; text-indent: 0em; margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; padding-top: 20px; padding-bottom: 8px; padding-left: 0px; padding-right: 0px;"><strong style="color: rgb(0, 0, 0); font-weight: bold; background-attachment: scroll; background-clip: border-box; background-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0); background-image: none; background-origin: padding-box; background-position-x: left; background-position-y: top; background-repeat: no-repeat; background-size: auto; width: auto; height: auto; margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; padding-top: 0px; padding-bottom: 0px; padding-left: 0px; padding-right: 0px; border-top-style: none; border-bottom-style: none; border-left-style: none; border-right-style: none; border-top-width: 3px; border-bottom-width: 3px; border-left-width: 3px; border-right-width: 3px; border-top-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.4); border-bottom-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.4); border-left-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.4); border-right-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.4); border-top-left-radius: 0px; border-top-right-radius: 0px; border-bottom-right-radius: 0px; border-bottom-left-radius: 0px;">为什么重要</strong>：
这篇文章直接回答了"情况明"怎么做——<strong style="color: rgb(0, 0, 0); font-weight: bold; background-attachment: scroll; background-clip: border-box; background-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0); background-image: none; background-origin: padding-box; background-position-x: left; background-position-y: top; background-repeat: no-repeat; background-size: auto; width: auto; height: auto; margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; padding-top: 0px; padding-bottom: 0px; padding-left: 0px; padding-right: 0px; border-top-style: none; border-bottom-style: none; border-left-style: none; border-right-style: none; border-top-width: 3px; border-bottom-width: 3px; border-left-width: 3px; border-right-width: 3px; border-top-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.4); border-bottom-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.4); border-left-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.4); border-right-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.4); border-top-left-radius: 0px; border-top-right-radius: 0px; border-bottom-right-radius: 0px; border-bottom-left-radius: 0px;">通过调查研究</strong>。研究研究，调查调查，一定要有目的有问题方向去搞。</p>
<p data-tool="mdnice编辑器" style="color: rgb(74, 74, 74); font-size: 16px; line-height: 1.8em; letter-spacing: 0.02em; text-align: left; text-indent: 0em; margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; padding-top: 20px; padding-bottom: 8px; padding-left: 0px; padding-right: 0px;">毛泽东在文中痛批那些不了解中国实际情况，只会背马列经典的教条主义者（"本本主义"），提出：</p>
<ul data-tool="mdnice编辑器" style="list-style-type: disc; margin-top: 8px; margin-bottom: 8px; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; padding-top: 0px; padding-bottom: 0px; padding-left: 25px; padding-right: 0px; color: rgb(0, 0, 0);">
<li><section style="margin-top: 5px; margin-bottom: 5px; color: rgb(1, 1, 1); font-size: 16px; line-height: 1.8em; letter-spacing: 0em; text-align: left; font-weight: normal;">调查研究是一切工作的基础</section></li><li><section style="margin-top: 5px; margin-bottom: 5px; color: rgb(1, 1, 1); font-size: 16px; line-height: 1.8em; letter-spacing: 0em; text-align: left; font-weight: normal;">"中国革命斗争的胜利要靠中国同志了解中国情况"</section></li></ul>
<hr data-tool="mdnice编辑器" style="margin-top: 10px; margin-bottom: 10px; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; padding-top: 0px; padding-bottom: 0px; padding-left: 0px; padding-right: 0px; border-top-style: none; border-bottom-style: none; border-left-style: none; border-right-style: none; border-top-width: 1px; border-bottom-width: 3px; border-left-width: 3px; border-right-width: 3px; border-top-color: rgb(0, 0, 0); border-bottom-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.4); border-left-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.4); border-right-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.4); border-top-left-radius: 0px; border-top-right-radius: 0px; border-bottom-right-radius: 0px; border-bottom-left-radius: 0px; background-attachment: scroll; background-clip: border-box; background-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0); background-image: linear-gradient(90deg, rgba(60, 112, 198, 0) 0%, rgba(60, 122, 198, 0.75) 50%, rgba(60, 122, 198, 0) 100%); background-origin: padding-box; background-position-x: left; background-position-y: top; background-repeat: no-repeat; background-size: auto; width: auto; height: 1px;">
<h4 data-tool="mdnice编辑器" style="margin-top: 30px; margin-bottom: 15px; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; padding-top: 0px; padding-bottom: 0px; padding-left: 0px; padding-right: 0px; display: block;"><span class="prefix" style="display: none;"></span><span class="content" style="font-size: 18px; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 1.5em; letter-spacing: 0em; text-align: left; font-weight: bold; display: block;">第二重要：《实践论》（1937年7月）</span><span class="suffix" style="display: none;"></span></h4>
<p data-tool="mdnice编辑器" style="color: rgb(74, 74, 74); font-size: 16px; line-height: 1.8em; letter-spacing: 0.02em; text-align: left; text-indent: 0em; margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; padding-top: 20px; padding-bottom: 8px; padding-left: 0px; padding-right: 0px;"><strong style="color: rgb(0, 0, 0); font-weight: bold; background-attachment: scroll; background-clip: border-box; background-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0); background-image: none; background-origin: padding-box; background-position-x: left; background-position-y: top; background-repeat: no-repeat; background-size: auto; width: auto; height: auto; margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; padding-top: 0px; padding-bottom: 0px; padding-left: 0px; padding-right: 0px; border-top-style: none; border-bottom-style: none; border-left-style: none; border-right-style: none; border-top-width: 3px; border-bottom-width: 3px; border-left-width: 3px; border-right-width: 3px; border-top-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.4); border-bottom-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.4); border-left-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.4); border-right-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.4); border-top-left-radius: 0px; border-top-right-radius: 0px; border-bottom-right-radius: 0px; border-bottom-left-radius: 0px;">副标题</strong>：论认识和实践的关系——知和行的关系</p>
<p data-tool="mdnice编辑器" style="color: rgb(74, 74, 74); font-size: 16px; line-height: 1.8em; letter-spacing: 0.02em; text-align: left; text-indent: 0em; margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; padding-top: 20px; padding-bottom: 8px; padding-left: 0px; padding-right: 0px;"><strong style="color: rgb(0, 0, 0); font-weight: bold; background-attachment: scroll; background-clip: border-box; background-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0); background-image: none; background-origin: padding-box; background-position-x: left; background-position-y: top; background-repeat: no-repeat; background-size: auto; width: auto; height: auto; margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; padding-top: 0px; padding-bottom: 0px; padding-left: 0px; padding-right: 0px; border-top-style: none; border-bottom-style: none; border-left-style: none; border-right-style: none; border-top-width: 3px; border-bottom-width: 3px; border-left-width: 3px; border-right-width: 3px; border-top-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.4); border-bottom-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.4); border-left-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.4); border-right-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.4); border-top-left-radius: 0px; border-top-right-radius: 0px; border-bottom-right-radius: 0px; border-bottom-left-radius: 0px;">核心思想</strong>：</p>
<blockquote class="custom-blockquote multiquote-1" data-tool="mdnice编辑器" style="margin-top: 20px; margin-bottom: 20px; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; padding-top: 10px; padding-bottom: 10px; padding-left: 20px; padding-right: 10px; border-top-style: none; border-bottom-style: none; border-left-style: none; border-right-style: none; border-top-width: 3px; border-bottom-width: 3px; border-left-width: 3px; border-right-width: 3px; border-top-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.4); border-bottom-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.4); border-left-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.4); border-right-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.4); border-top-left-radius: 0px; border-top-right-radius: 0px; border-bottom-right-radius: 0px; border-bottom-left-radius: 0px; background-attachment: scroll; background-clip: border-box; background-color: rgb(239, 239, 239); background-image: none; background-origin: padding-box; background-position-x: left; background-position-y: top; background-repeat: no-repeat; background-size: auto; width: auto; height: auto; box-shadow: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0) 0px 0px 0px 0px; display: block; overflow-x: auto; overflow-y: auto;"><span style="display: none; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); font-size: 16px; line-height: 1.5em; letter-spacing: 0em; text-align: left; font-weight: normal;"></span>
<p style="text-indent: 0em; padding-top: 20px; padding-bottom: 8px; padding-left: 0px; padding-right: 0px; color: rgb(89, 89, 89); font-size: 16px; line-height: 1.8em; letter-spacing: 0em; text-align: left; font-weight: normal; margin-top: 0px; margin-right: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; margin-left: 0px;">"实践、认识、再实践、再认识，这种形式，循环往复以至无穷，而实践和认识之每一循环的内容，都比较地进到了高一级的程度。"</p>
</blockquote>
<p data-tool="mdnice编辑器" style="color: rgb(74, 74, 74); font-size: 16px; line-height: 1.8em; letter-spacing: 0.02em; text-align: left; text-indent: 0em; margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; padding-top: 20px; padding-bottom: 8px; padding-left: 0px; padding-right: 0px;"><strong style="color: rgb(0, 0, 0); font-weight: bold; background-attachment: scroll; background-clip: border-box; background-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0); background-image: none; background-origin: padding-box; background-position-x: left; background-position-y: top; background-repeat: no-repeat; background-size: auto; width: auto; height: auto; margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; padding-top: 0px; padding-bottom: 0px; padding-left: 0px; padding-right: 0px; border-top-style: none; border-bottom-style: none; border-left-style: none; border-right-style: none; border-top-width: 3px; border-bottom-width: 3px; border-left-width: 3px; border-right-width: 3px; border-top-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.4); border-bottom-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.4); border-left-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.4); border-right-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.4); border-top-left-radius: 0px; border-top-right-radius: 0px; border-bottom-right-radius: 0px; border-bottom-left-radius: 0px;">为什么重要</strong>：
这篇文章从哲学高度论述了"情况明"的认识论基础：</p>
<ul data-tool="mdnice编辑器" style="list-style-type: disc; margin-top: 8px; margin-bottom: 8px; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; padding-top: 0px; padding-bottom: 0px; padding-left: 25px; padding-right: 0px; color: rgb(0, 0, 0);">
<li><section style="margin-top: 5px; margin-bottom: 5px; color: rgb(1, 1, 1); font-size: 16px; line-height: 1.8em; letter-spacing: 0em; text-align: left; font-weight: normal;">认识来自实践（不是坐在屋里想出来的）</section></li><li><section style="margin-top: 5px; margin-bottom: 5px; color: rgb(1, 1, 1); font-size: 16px; line-height: 1.8em; letter-spacing: 0em; text-align: left; font-weight: normal;">认识要回到实践中检验（不能纸上谈兵）</section></li><li><section style="margin-top: 5px; margin-bottom: 5px; color: rgb(1, 1, 1); font-size: 16px; line-height: 1.8em; letter-spacing: 0em; text-align: left; font-weight: normal;">要反复循环（情况是动态的，要持续调查）</section></li></ul>
<p data-tool="mdnice编辑器" style="color: rgb(74, 74, 74); font-size: 16px; line-height: 1.8em; letter-spacing: 0.02em; text-align: left; text-indent: 0em; margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; padding-top: 20px; padding-bottom: 8px; padding-left: 0px; padding-right: 0px;"><strong style="color: rgb(0, 0, 0); font-weight: bold; background-attachment: scroll; background-clip: border-box; background-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0); background-image: none; background-origin: padding-box; background-position-x: left; background-position-y: top; background-repeat: no-repeat; background-size: auto; width: auto; height: auto; margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; padding-top: 0px; padding-bottom: 0px; padding-left: 0px; padding-right: 0px; border-top-style: none; border-bottom-style: none; border-left-style: none; border-right-style: none; border-top-width: 3px; border-bottom-width: 3px; border-left-width: 3px; border-right-width: 3px; border-top-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.4); border-bottom-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.4); border-left-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.4); border-right-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.4); border-top-left-radius: 0px; border-top-right-radius: 0px; border-bottom-right-radius: 0px; border-bottom-left-radius: 0px;">对应九字真言</strong>：</p>
<ul data-tool="mdnice编辑器" style="list-style-type: disc; margin-top: 8px; margin-bottom: 8px; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; padding-top: 0px; padding-bottom: 0px; padding-left: 25px; padding-right: 0px; color: rgb(0, 0, 0);">
<li><section style="margin-top: 5px; margin-bottom: 5px; color: rgb(1, 1, 1); font-size: 16px; line-height: 1.8em; letter-spacing: 0em; text-align: left; font-weight: normal;">情况明 = 通过实践获得正确认识</section></li><li><section style="margin-top: 5px; margin-bottom: 5px; color: rgb(1, 1, 1); font-size: 16px; line-height: 1.8em; letter-spacing: 0em; text-align: left; font-weight: normal;">方法对 = 把正确认识用于指导实践</section></li></ul>
<hr data-tool="mdnice编辑器" style="margin-top: 10px; margin-bottom: 10px; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; padding-top: 0px; padding-bottom: 0px; padding-left: 0px; padding-right: 0px; border-top-style: none; border-bottom-style: none; border-left-style: none; border-right-style: none; border-top-width: 1px; border-bottom-width: 3px; border-left-width: 3px; border-right-width: 3px; border-top-color: rgb(0, 0, 0); border-bottom-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.4); border-left-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.4); border-right-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.4); border-top-left-radius: 0px; border-top-right-radius: 0px; border-bottom-right-radius: 0px; border-bottom-left-radius: 0px; background-attachment: scroll; background-clip: border-box; background-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0); background-image: linear-gradient(90deg, rgba(60, 112, 198, 0) 0%, rgba(60, 122, 198, 0.75) 50%, rgba(60, 122, 198, 0) 100%); background-origin: padding-box; background-position-x: left; background-position-y: top; background-repeat: no-repeat; background-size: auto; width: auto; height: 1px;">
<h4 data-tool="mdnice编辑器" style="margin-top: 30px; margin-bottom: 15px; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; padding-top: 0px; padding-bottom: 0px; padding-left: 0px; padding-right: 0px; display: block;"><span class="prefix" style="display: none;"></span><span class="content" style="font-size: 18px; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 1.5em; letter-spacing: 0em; text-align: left; font-weight: bold; display: block;">第三重要：《矛盾论》（1937年8月）</span><span class="suffix" style="display: none;"></span></h4>
<p data-tool="mdnice编辑器" style="color: rgb(74, 74, 74); font-size: 16px; line-height: 1.8em; letter-spacing: 0.02em; text-align: left; text-indent: 0em; margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; padding-top: 20px; padding-bottom: 8px; padding-left: 0px; padding-right: 0px;"><strong style="color: rgb(0, 0, 0); font-weight: bold; background-attachment: scroll; background-clip: border-box; background-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0); background-image: none; background-origin: padding-box; background-position-x: left; background-position-y: top; background-repeat: no-repeat; background-size: auto; width: auto; height: auto; margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; padding-top: 0px; padding-bottom: 0px; padding-left: 0px; padding-right: 0px; border-top-style: none; border-bottom-style: none; border-left-style: none; border-right-style: none; border-top-width: 3px; border-bottom-width: 3px; border-left-width: 3px; border-right-width: 3px; border-top-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.4); border-bottom-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.4); border-left-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.4); border-right-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.4); border-top-left-radius: 0px; border-top-right-radius: 0px; border-bottom-right-radius: 0px; border-bottom-left-radius: 0px;">核心思想</strong>：</p>
<blockquote class="custom-blockquote multiquote-1" data-tool="mdnice编辑器" style="margin-top: 20px; margin-bottom: 20px; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; padding-top: 10px; padding-bottom: 10px; padding-left: 20px; padding-right: 10px; border-top-style: none; border-bottom-style: none; border-left-style: none; border-right-style: none; border-top-width: 3px; border-bottom-width: 3px; border-left-width: 3px; border-right-width: 3px; border-top-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.4); border-bottom-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.4); border-left-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.4); border-right-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.4); border-top-left-radius: 0px; border-top-right-radius: 0px; border-bottom-right-radius: 0px; border-bottom-left-radius: 0px; background-attachment: scroll; background-clip: border-box; background-color: rgb(239, 239, 239); background-image: none; background-origin: padding-box; background-position-x: left; background-position-y: top; background-repeat: no-repeat; background-size: auto; width: auto; height: auto; box-shadow: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0) 0px 0px 0px 0px; display: block; overflow-x: auto; overflow-y: auto;"><span style="display: none; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); font-size: 16px; line-height: 1.5em; letter-spacing: 0em; text-align: left; font-weight: normal;"></span>
<p style="text-indent: 0em; padding-top: 20px; padding-bottom: 8px; padding-left: 0px; padding-right: 0px; color: rgb(89, 89, 89); font-size: 16px; line-height: 1.8em; letter-spacing: 0em; text-align: left; font-weight: normal; margin-top: 0px; margin-right: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; margin-left: 0px;">"研究问题，忌带主观性、片面性和表面性。"<br>
"不同质的矛盾，只有用不同质的方法才能解决。"</p>
</blockquote>
<p data-tool="mdnice编辑器" style="color: rgb(74, 74, 74); font-size: 16px; line-height: 1.8em; letter-spacing: 0.02em; text-align: left; text-indent: 0em; margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; padding-top: 20px; padding-bottom: 8px; padding-left: 0px; padding-right: 0px;"><strong style="color: rgb(0, 0, 0); font-weight: bold; background-attachment: scroll; background-clip: border-box; background-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0); background-image: none; background-origin: padding-box; background-position-x: left; background-position-y: top; background-repeat: no-repeat; background-size: auto; width: auto; height: auto; margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; padding-top: 0px; padding-bottom: 0px; padding-left: 0px; padding-right: 0px; border-top-style: none; border-bottom-style: none; border-left-style: none; border-right-style: none; border-top-width: 3px; border-bottom-width: 3px; border-left-width: 3px; border-right-width: 3px; border-top-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.4); border-bottom-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.4); border-left-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.4); border-right-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.4); border-top-left-radius: 0px; border-top-right-radius: 0px; border-bottom-right-radius: 0px; border-bottom-left-radius: 0px;">为什么重要</strong>：
这篇文章教你"怎么把情况看明白"：</p>
<ul data-tool="mdnice编辑器" style="list-style-type: disc; margin-top: 8px; margin-bottom: 8px; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; padding-top: 0px; padding-bottom: 0px; padding-left: 25px; padding-right: 0px; color: rgb(0, 0, 0);">
<li><section style="margin-top: 5px; margin-bottom: 5px; color: rgb(1, 1, 1); font-size: 16px; line-height: 1.8em; letter-spacing: 0em; text-align: left; font-weight: normal;">分清主要矛盾和次要矛盾</section></li><li><section style="margin-top: 5px; margin-bottom: 5px; color: rgb(1, 1, 1); font-size: 16px; line-height: 1.8em; letter-spacing: 0em; text-align: left; font-weight: normal;">分清矛盾的主要方面和次要方面</section></li><li><section style="margin-top: 5px; margin-bottom: 5px; color: rgb(1, 1, 1); font-size: 16px; line-height: 1.8em; letter-spacing: 0em; text-align: left; font-weight: normal;">具体问题具体分析（不能一刀切）</section></li></ul>
<p data-tool="mdnice编辑器" style="color: rgb(74, 74, 74); font-size: 16px; line-height: 1.8em; letter-spacing: 0.02em; text-align: left; text-indent: 0em; margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; padding-top: 20px; padding-bottom: 8px; padding-left: 0px; padding-right: 0px;">**文中引用了"宋江三打祝家庄"**：</p>
<blockquote class="custom-blockquote multiquote-1" data-tool="mdnice编辑器" style="margin-top: 20px; margin-bottom: 20px; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; padding-top: 10px; padding-bottom: 10px; padding-left: 20px; padding-right: 10px; border-top-style: none; border-bottom-style: none; border-left-style: none; border-right-style: none; border-top-width: 3px; border-bottom-width: 3px; border-left-width: 3px; border-right-width: 3px; border-top-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.4); border-bottom-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.4); border-left-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.4); border-right-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.4); border-top-left-radius: 0px; border-top-right-radius: 0px; border-bottom-right-radius: 0px; border-bottom-left-radius: 0px; background-attachment: scroll; background-clip: border-box; background-color: rgb(239, 239, 239); background-image: none; background-origin: padding-box; background-position-x: left; background-position-y: top; background-repeat: no-repeat; background-size: auto; width: auto; height: auto; box-shadow: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0) 0px 0px 0px 0px; display: block; overflow-x: auto; overflow-y: auto;"><span style="display: none; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); font-size: 16px; line-height: 1.5em; letter-spacing: 0em; text-align: left; font-weight: normal;"></span>
<p style="text-indent: 0em; padding-top: 20px; padding-bottom: 8px; padding-left: 0px; padding-right: 0px; color: rgb(89, 89, 89); font-size: 16px; line-height: 1.8em; letter-spacing: 0em; text-align: left; font-weight: normal; margin-top: 0px; margin-right: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; margin-left: 0px;">"《水浒传》上宋江三打祝家庄，两次都因情况不明，方法不对，打败了。后来改变方法，从调查情形入手，于是熟悉了盘陀路，拆散了李家庄、扈家庄和祝家庄的联盟，并且布置了藏在敌人营盘里的伏兵，用了和外国故事中所说木马计相像的方法，第三次就打了胜仗。"</p>
</blockquote>
<p data-tool="mdnice编辑器" style="color: rgb(74, 74, 74); font-size: 16px; line-height: 1.8em; letter-spacing: 0.02em; text-align: left; text-indent: 0em; margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; padding-top: 20px; padding-bottom: 8px; padding-left: 0px; padding-right: 0px;"><strong style="color: rgb(0, 0, 0); font-weight: bold; background-attachment: scroll; background-clip: border-box; background-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0); background-image: none; background-origin: padding-box; background-position-x: left; background-position-y: top; background-repeat: no-repeat; background-size: auto; width: auto; height: auto; margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; padding-top: 0px; padding-bottom: 0px; padding-left: 0px; padding-right: 0px; border-top-style: none; border-bottom-style: none; border-left-style: none; border-right-style: none; border-top-width: 3px; border-bottom-width: 3px; border-left-width: 3px; border-right-width: 3px; border-top-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.4); border-bottom-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.4); border-left-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.4); border-right-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.4); border-top-left-radius: 0px; border-top-right-radius: 0px; border-bottom-right-radius: 0px; border-bottom-left-radius: 0px;">《矛盾论》里已经明确说了"情况不明，方法不对"！</strong></p>
<hr data-tool="mdnice编辑器" style="margin-top: 10px; margin-bottom: 10px; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; padding-top: 0px; padding-bottom: 0px; padding-left: 0px; padding-right: 0px; border-top-style: none; border-bottom-style: none; border-left-style: none; border-right-style: none; border-top-width: 1px; border-bottom-width: 3px; border-left-width: 3px; border-right-width: 3px; border-top-color: rgb(0, 0, 0); border-bottom-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.4); border-left-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.4); border-right-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.4); border-top-left-radius: 0px; border-top-right-radius: 0px; border-bottom-right-radius: 0px; border-bottom-left-radius: 0px; background-attachment: scroll; background-clip: border-box; background-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0); background-image: linear-gradient(90deg, rgba(60, 112, 198, 0) 0%, rgba(60, 122, 198, 0.75) 50%, rgba(60, 122, 198, 0) 100%); background-origin: padding-box; background-position-x: left; background-position-y: top; background-repeat: no-repeat; background-size: auto; width: auto; height: 1px;">
<h3 data-tool="mdnice编辑器" style="margin-top: 30px; margin-bottom: 15px; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; padding-top: 0px; padding-bottom: 0px; padding-left: 0px; padding-right: 0px; align-items: unset; background-attachment: scroll; background-clip: border-box; background-color: transparent; background-image: none; background-origin: padding-box; background-position-x: 0%; background-position-y: 0%; background-repeat: no-repeat; background-size: auto; border-top-style: none; border-bottom-style: none; border-left-style: none; border-right-style: none; border-top-width: 1px; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-left-width: 1px; border-right-width: 1px; border-top-color: rgb(0, 0, 0); border-bottom-color: rgb(0, 0, 0); border-left-color: rgb(0, 0, 0); border-right-color: rgb(0, 0, 0); border-top-left-radius: 0px; border-top-right-radius: 0px; border-bottom-left-radius: 0px; border-bottom-right-radius: 0px; box-shadow: none; display: block; flex-direction: unset; float: unset; height: auto; justify-content: unset; line-height: 1.5em; overflow-x: unset; overflow-y: unset; position: relative; text-align: left; text-shadow: none; transform: none; width: auto; -webkit-box-reflect: unset;"><span style="background-attachment: scroll; background-clip: border-box; background-color: transparent; background-image: url('https://files.mdnice.com/mountain_1.png'); background-origin: padding-box; background-position-x: 0%; background-position-y: 0%; background-repeat: no-repeat; background-size: 15px 15px; width: 15px; height: 15px; align-items: unset; border-top-style: none; border-bottom-style: none; border-left-style: none; border-right-style: none; border-top-width: 1px; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-left-width: 1px; border-right-width: 1px; border-top-color: rgb(0, 0, 0); border-bottom-color: rgb(0, 0, 0); border-left-color: rgb(0, 0, 0); border-right-color: rgb(0, 0, 0); border-top-left-radius: 0px; border-top-right-radius: 0px; border-bottom-left-radius: 0px; border-bottom-right-radius: 0px; box-shadow: none; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); display: inline-block; font-size: 22px; font-weight: bold; flex-direction: unset; float: unset; justify-content: unset; letter-spacing: 0px; line-height: 1.5em; margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: -2px; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; overflow-x: unset; overflow-y: unset; padding-top: 0px; padding-bottom: 0px; padding-left: 0px; padding-right: 0px; position: relative; text-align: left; text-indent: 0em; text-shadow: none; transform: none; -webkit-box-reflect: unset;"></span><span class="prefix" style="display: none;"></span><span class="content" style="font-size: 16px; color: rgb(60, 112, 198); line-height: 1.5em; letter-spacing: 0em; align-items: unset; background-attachment: scroll; background-clip: border-box; background-color: transparent; background-image: none; background-origin: padding-box; background-position-x: 0%; background-position-y: 0%; background-repeat: no-repeat; background-size: auto; border-top-style: none; border-bottom-style: none; border-left-style: none; border-right-style: none; border-top-width: 1px; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-left-width: 1px; border-right-width: 1px; border-top-color: rgb(0, 0, 0); border-bottom-color: rgb(0, 0, 0); border-left-color: rgb(0, 0, 0); border-right-color: rgb(0, 0, 0); border-top-left-radius: 0px; border-top-right-radius: 0px; border-bottom-left-radius: 0px; border-bottom-right-radius: 0px; box-shadow: none; display: inline-block; font-weight: bold; flex-direction: unset; float: unset; height: auto; justify-content: unset; margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; margin-left: 8px; margin-right: 0px; overflow-x: unset; overflow-y: unset; padding-top: 0px; padding-bottom: 0px; padding-left: 0px; padding-right: 0px; position: relative; text-align: left; text-indent: 0em; text-shadow: none; transform: none; width: auto; -webkit-box-reflect: unset;">2. 【决心大】的思想源头</span><span class="suffix" style="display: none;"></span></h3>
<h4 data-tool="mdnice编辑器" style="margin-top: 30px; margin-bottom: 15px; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; padding-top: 0px; padding-bottom: 0px; padding-left: 0px; padding-right: 0px; display: block;"><span class="prefix" style="display: none;"></span><span class="content" style="font-size: 18px; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 1.5em; letter-spacing: 0em; text-align: left; font-weight: bold; display: block;">最核心的文章：《论持久战》（1938年5月）</span><span class="suffix" style="display: none;"></span></h4>
<p data-tool="mdnice编辑器" style="color: rgb(74, 74, 74); font-size: 16px; line-height: 1.8em; letter-spacing: 0.02em; text-align: left; text-indent: 0em; margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; padding-top: 20px; padding-bottom: 8px; padding-left: 0px; padding-right: 0px;"><strong style="color: rgb(0, 0, 0); font-weight: bold; background-attachment: scroll; background-clip: border-box; background-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0); background-image: none; background-origin: padding-box; background-position-x: left; background-position-y: top; background-repeat: no-repeat; background-size: auto; width: auto; height: auto; margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; padding-top: 0px; padding-bottom: 0px; padding-left: 0px; padding-right: 0px; border-top-style: none; border-bottom-style: none; border-left-style: none; border-right-style: none; border-top-width: 3px; border-bottom-width: 3px; border-left-width: 3px; border-right-width: 3px; border-top-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.4); border-bottom-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.4); border-left-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.4); border-right-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.4); border-top-left-radius: 0px; border-top-right-radius: 0px; border-bottom-right-radius: 0px; border-bottom-left-radius: 0px;">背景</strong>：抗战初期，国内有"亡国论"和"速胜论"两种错误思潮</p>
<p data-tool="mdnice编辑器" style="color: rgb(74, 74, 74); font-size: 16px; line-height: 1.8em; letter-spacing: 0.02em; text-align: left; text-indent: 0em; margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; padding-top: 20px; padding-bottom: 8px; padding-left: 0px; padding-right: 0px;"><strong style="color: rgb(0, 0, 0); font-weight: bold; background-attachment: scroll; background-clip: border-box; background-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0); background-image: none; background-origin: padding-box; background-position-x: left; background-position-y: top; background-repeat: no-repeat; background-size: auto; width: auto; height: auto; margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; padding-top: 0px; padding-bottom: 0px; padding-left: 0px; padding-right: 0px; border-top-style: none; border-bottom-style: none; border-left-style: none; border-right-style: none; border-top-width: 3px; border-bottom-width: 3px; border-left-width: 3px; border-right-width: 3px; border-top-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.4); border-bottom-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.4); border-left-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.4); border-right-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.4); border-top-left-radius: 0px; border-top-right-radius: 0px; border-bottom-right-radius: 0px; border-bottom-left-radius: 0px;">核心思想</strong>：
毛泽东通过深入分析中日双方的基本特点，得出结论：</p>
<ul data-tool="mdnice编辑器" style="list-style-type: disc; margin-top: 8px; margin-bottom: 8px; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; padding-top: 0px; padding-bottom: 0px; padding-left: 25px; padding-right: 0px; color: rgb(0, 0, 0);">
<li><section style="margin-top: 5px; margin-bottom: 5px; color: rgb(1, 1, 1); font-size: 16px; line-height: 1.8em; letter-spacing: 0em; text-align: left; font-weight: normal;">日本必败</section></li><li><section style="margin-top: 5px; margin-bottom: 5px; color: rgb(1, 1, 1); font-size: 16px; line-height: 1.8em; letter-spacing: 0em; text-align: left; font-weight: normal;">中国必胜</section></li><li><section style="margin-top: 5px; margin-bottom: 5px; color: rgb(1, 1, 1); font-size: 16px; line-height: 1.8em; letter-spacing: 0em; text-align: left; font-weight: normal;">但需要持久战（三个阶段：防御、相持、反攻）</section></li></ul>
<p data-tool="mdnice编辑器" style="color: rgb(74, 74, 74); font-size: 16px; line-height: 1.8em; letter-spacing: 0.02em; text-align: left; text-indent: 0em; margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; padding-top: 20px; padding-bottom: 8px; padding-left: 0px; padding-right: 0px;">**为什么这是"决心大"**：
因为毛泽东在最艰难的时刻（日军攻占大半个中国），通过对"情况"的深刻分析，给出了"必胜"的判断，这给了全国人民坚持下去的信心。</p>
<p data-tool="mdnice编辑器" style="color: rgb(74, 74, 74); font-size: 16px; line-height: 1.8em; letter-spacing: 0.02em; text-align: left; text-indent: 0em; margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; padding-top: 20px; padding-bottom: 8px; padding-left: 0px; padding-right: 0px;"><strong style="color: rgb(0, 0, 0); font-weight: bold; background-attachment: scroll; background-clip: border-box; background-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0); background-image: none; background-origin: padding-box; background-position-x: left; background-position-y: top; background-repeat: no-repeat; background-size: auto; width: auto; height: auto; margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; padding-top: 0px; padding-bottom: 0px; padding-left: 0px; padding-right: 0px; border-top-style: none; border-bottom-style: none; border-left-style: none; border-right-style: none; border-top-width: 3px; border-bottom-width: 3px; border-left-width: 3px; border-right-width: 3px; border-top-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.4); border-bottom-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.4); border-left-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.4); border-right-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.4); border-top-left-radius: 0px; border-top-right-radius: 0px; border-bottom-right-radius: 0px; border-bottom-left-radius: 0px;">对应九字真言</strong>：</p>
<blockquote class="custom-blockquote multiquote-1" data-tool="mdnice编辑器" style="margin-top: 20px; margin-bottom: 20px; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; padding-top: 10px; padding-bottom: 10px; padding-left: 20px; padding-right: 10px; border-top-style: none; border-bottom-style: none; border-left-style: none; border-right-style: none; border-top-width: 3px; border-bottom-width: 3px; border-left-width: 3px; border-right-width: 3px; border-top-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.4); border-bottom-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.4); border-left-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.4); border-right-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.4); border-top-left-radius: 0px; border-top-right-radius: 0px; border-bottom-right-radius: 0px; border-bottom-left-radius: 0px; background-attachment: scroll; background-clip: border-box; background-color: rgb(239, 239, 239); background-image: none; background-origin: padding-box; background-position-x: left; background-position-y: top; background-repeat: no-repeat; background-size: auto; width: auto; height: auto; box-shadow: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0) 0px 0px 0px 0px; display: block; overflow-x: auto; overflow-y: auto;"><span style="display: none; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); font-size: 16px; line-height: 1.5em; letter-spacing: 0em; text-align: left; font-weight: normal;"></span>
<p style="text-indent: 0em; padding-top: 20px; padding-bottom: 8px; padding-left: 0px; padding-right: 0px; color: rgb(89, 89, 89); font-size: 16px; line-height: 1.8em; letter-spacing: 0em; text-align: left; font-weight: normal; margin-top: 0px; margin-right: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; margin-left: 0px;">"情况越明，决心越大。"</p>
</blockquote>
<p data-tool="mdnice编辑器" style="color: rgb(74, 74, 74); font-size: 16px; line-height: 1.8em; letter-spacing: 0.02em; text-align: left; text-indent: 0em; margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; padding-top: 20px; padding-bottom: 8px; padding-left: 0px; padding-right: 0px;">毛泽东正是因为把中日双方的情况分析透了（情况明），所以才敢下"持久战必胜"的结论（决心大）。</p>
<hr data-tool="mdnice编辑器" style="margin-top: 10px; margin-bottom: 10px; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; padding-top: 0px; padding-bottom: 0px; padding-left: 0px; padding-right: 0px; border-top-style: none; border-bottom-style: none; border-left-style: none; border-right-style: none; border-top-width: 1px; border-bottom-width: 3px; border-left-width: 3px; border-right-width: 3px; border-top-color: rgb(0, 0, 0); border-bottom-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.4); border-left-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.4); border-right-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.4); border-top-left-radius: 0px; border-top-right-radius: 0px; border-bottom-right-radius: 0px; border-bottom-left-radius: 0px; background-attachment: scroll; background-clip: border-box; background-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0); background-image: linear-gradient(90deg, rgba(60, 112, 198, 0) 0%, rgba(60, 122, 198, 0.75) 50%, rgba(60, 122, 198, 0) 100%); background-origin: padding-box; background-position-x: left; background-position-y: top; background-repeat: no-repeat; background-size: auto; width: auto; height: 1px;">
<h4 data-tool="mdnice编辑器" style="margin-top: 30px; margin-bottom: 15px; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; padding-top: 0px; padding-bottom: 0px; padding-left: 0px; padding-right: 0px; display: block;"><span class="prefix" style="display: none;"></span><span class="content" style="font-size: 18px; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 1.5em; letter-spacing: 0em; text-align: left; font-weight: bold; display: block;">第二重要：《愚公移山》（1945年6月）</span><span class="suffix" style="display: none;"></span></h4>
<p data-tool="mdnice编辑器" style="color: rgb(74, 74, 74); font-size: 16px; line-height: 1.8em; letter-spacing: 0.02em; text-align: left; text-indent: 0em; margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; padding-top: 20px; padding-bottom: 8px; padding-left: 0px; padding-right: 0px;"><strong style="color: rgb(0, 0, 0); font-weight: bold; background-attachment: scroll; background-clip: border-box; background-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0); background-image: none; background-origin: padding-box; background-position-x: left; background-position-y: top; background-repeat: no-repeat; background-size: auto; width: auto; height: auto; margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; padding-top: 0px; padding-bottom: 0px; padding-left: 0px; padding-right: 0px; border-top-style: none; border-bottom-style: none; border-left-style: none; border-right-style: none; border-top-width: 3px; border-bottom-width: 3px; border-left-width: 3px; border-right-width: 3px; border-top-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.4); border-bottom-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.4); border-left-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.4); border-right-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.4); border-top-left-radius: 0px; border-top-right-radius: 0px; border-bottom-right-radius: 0px; border-bottom-left-radius: 0px;">背景</strong>：七大闭幕词</p>
<p data-tool="mdnice编辑器" style="color: rgb(74, 74, 74); font-size: 16px; line-height: 1.8em; letter-spacing: 0.02em; text-align: left; text-indent: 0em; margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; padding-top: 20px; padding-bottom: 8px; padding-left: 0px; padding-right: 0px;"><strong style="color: rgb(0, 0, 0); font-weight: bold; background-attachment: scroll; background-clip: border-box; background-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0); background-image: none; background-origin: padding-box; background-position-x: left; background-position-y: top; background-repeat: no-repeat; background-size: auto; width: auto; height: auto; margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; padding-top: 0px; padding-bottom: 0px; padding-left: 0px; padding-right: 0px; border-top-style: none; border-bottom-style: none; border-left-style: none; border-right-style: none; border-top-width: 3px; border-bottom-width: 3px; border-left-width: 3px; border-right-width: 3px; border-top-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.4); border-bottom-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.4); border-left-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.4); border-right-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.4); border-top-left-radius: 0px; border-top-right-radius: 0px; border-bottom-right-radius: 0px; border-bottom-left-radius: 0px;">核心思想</strong>：</p>
<blockquote class="custom-blockquote multiquote-1" data-tool="mdnice编辑器" style="margin-top: 20px; margin-bottom: 20px; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; padding-top: 10px; padding-bottom: 10px; padding-left: 20px; padding-right: 10px; border-top-style: none; border-bottom-style: none; border-left-style: none; border-right-style: none; border-top-width: 3px; border-bottom-width: 3px; border-left-width: 3px; border-right-width: 3px; border-top-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.4); border-bottom-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.4); border-left-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.4); border-right-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.4); border-top-left-radius: 0px; border-top-right-radius: 0px; border-bottom-right-radius: 0px; border-bottom-left-radius: 0px; background-attachment: scroll; background-clip: border-box; background-color: rgb(239, 239, 239); background-image: none; background-origin: padding-box; background-position-x: left; background-position-y: top; background-repeat: no-repeat; background-size: auto; width: auto; height: auto; box-shadow: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0) 0px 0px 0px 0px; display: block; overflow-x: auto; overflow-y: auto;"><span style="display: none; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); font-size: 16px; line-height: 1.5em; letter-spacing: 0em; text-align: left; font-weight: normal;"></span>
<p style="text-indent: 0em; padding-top: 20px; padding-bottom: 8px; padding-left: 0px; padding-right: 0px; color: rgb(89, 89, 89); font-size: 16px; line-height: 1.8em; letter-spacing: 0em; text-align: left; font-weight: normal; margin-top: 0px; margin-right: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; margin-left: 0px;">"现在也有两座压在中国人民头上的大山，一座叫做帝国主义，一座叫做封建主义。中国共产党早就下了决心，要挖掉这两座山。我们一定要坚持下去，一定要不断地工作，我们也会感动上帝的。这个上帝不是别人，就是全中国的人民大众。"</p>
</blockquote>
<p data-tool="mdnice编辑器" style="color: rgb(74, 74, 74); font-size: 16px; line-height: 1.8em; letter-spacing: 0.02em; text-align: left; text-indent: 0em; margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; padding-top: 20px; padding-bottom: 8px; padding-left: 0px; padding-right: 0px;">**为什么这是"决心大"**：
这篇讲话虽然简短，但体现了一种"明知山有虎，偏向虎山行"的决心——但这个决心不是盲目的，而是基于对"人民大众"力量的深刻认识（情况明）。</p>
<hr data-tool="mdnice编辑器" style="margin-top: 10px; margin-bottom: 10px; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; padding-top: 0px; padding-bottom: 0px; padding-left: 0px; padding-right: 0px; border-top-style: none; border-bottom-style: none; border-left-style: none; border-right-style: none; border-top-width: 1px; border-bottom-width: 3px; border-left-width: 3px; border-right-width: 3px; border-top-color: rgb(0, 0, 0); border-bottom-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.4); border-left-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.4); border-right-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.4); border-top-left-radius: 0px; border-top-right-radius: 0px; border-bottom-right-radius: 0px; border-bottom-left-radius: 0px; background-attachment: scroll; background-clip: border-box; background-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0); background-image: linear-gradient(90deg, rgba(60, 112, 198, 0) 0%, rgba(60, 122, 198, 0.75) 50%, rgba(60, 122, 198, 0) 100%); background-origin: padding-box; background-position-x: left; background-position-y: top; background-repeat: no-repeat; background-size: auto; width: auto; height: 1px;">
<h3 data-tool="mdnice编辑器" style="margin-top: 30px; margin-bottom: 15px; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; padding-top: 0px; padding-bottom: 0px; padding-left: 0px; padding-right: 0px; align-items: unset; background-attachment: scroll; background-clip: border-box; background-color: transparent; background-image: none; background-origin: padding-box; background-position-x: 0%; background-position-y: 0%; background-repeat: no-repeat; background-size: auto; border-top-style: none; border-bottom-style: none; border-left-style: none; border-right-style: none; border-top-width: 1px; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-left-width: 1px; border-right-width: 1px; border-top-color: rgb(0, 0, 0); border-bottom-color: rgb(0, 0, 0); border-left-color: rgb(0, 0, 0); border-right-color: rgb(0, 0, 0); border-top-left-radius: 0px; border-top-right-radius: 0px; border-bottom-left-radius: 0px; border-bottom-right-radius: 0px; box-shadow: none; display: block; flex-direction: unset; float: unset; height: auto; justify-content: unset; line-height: 1.5em; overflow-x: unset; overflow-y: unset; position: relative; text-align: left; text-shadow: none; transform: none; width: auto; -webkit-box-reflect: unset;"><span style="background-attachment: scroll; background-clip: border-box; background-color: transparent; background-image: url('https://files.mdnice.com/mountain_1.png'); background-origin: padding-box; background-position-x: 0%; background-position-y: 0%; background-repeat: no-repeat; background-size: 15px 15px; width: 15px; height: 15px; align-items: unset; border-top-style: none; border-bottom-style: none; border-left-style: none; border-right-style: none; border-top-width: 1px; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-left-width: 1px; border-right-width: 1px; border-top-color: rgb(0, 0, 0); border-bottom-color: rgb(0, 0, 0); border-left-color: rgb(0, 0, 0); border-right-color: rgb(0, 0, 0); border-top-left-radius: 0px; border-top-right-radius: 0px; border-bottom-left-radius: 0px; border-bottom-right-radius: 0px; box-shadow: none; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); display: inline-block; font-size: 22px; font-weight: bold; flex-direction: unset; float: unset; justify-content: unset; letter-spacing: 0px; line-height: 1.5em; margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: -2px; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; overflow-x: unset; overflow-y: unset; padding-top: 0px; padding-bottom: 0px; padding-left: 0px; padding-right: 0px; position: relative; text-align: left; text-indent: 0em; text-shadow: none; transform: none; -webkit-box-reflect: unset;"></span><span class="prefix" style="display: none;"></span><span class="content" style="font-size: 16px; color: rgb(60, 112, 198); line-height: 1.5em; letter-spacing: 0em; align-items: unset; background-attachment: scroll; background-clip: border-box; background-color: transparent; background-image: none; background-origin: padding-box; background-position-x: 0%; background-position-y: 0%; background-repeat: no-repeat; background-size: auto; border-top-style: none; border-bottom-style: none; border-left-style: none; border-right-style: none; border-top-width: 1px; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-left-width: 1px; border-right-width: 1px; border-top-color: rgb(0, 0, 0); border-bottom-color: rgb(0, 0, 0); border-left-color: rgb(0, 0, 0); border-right-color: rgb(0, 0, 0); border-top-left-radius: 0px; border-top-right-radius: 0px; border-bottom-left-radius: 0px; border-bottom-right-radius: 0px; box-shadow: none; display: inline-block; font-weight: bold; flex-direction: unset; float: unset; height: auto; justify-content: unset; margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; margin-left: 8px; margin-right: 0px; overflow-x: unset; overflow-y: unset; padding-top: 0px; padding-bottom: 0px; padding-left: 0px; padding-right: 0px; position: relative; text-align: left; text-indent: 0em; text-shadow: none; transform: none; width: auto; -webkit-box-reflect: unset;">3. 【方法对】的思想源头</span><span class="suffix" style="display: none;"></span></h3>
<h4 data-tool="mdnice编辑器" style="margin-top: 30px; margin-bottom: 15px; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; padding-top: 0px; padding-bottom: 0px; padding-left: 0px; padding-right: 0px; display: block;"><span class="prefix" style="display: none;"></span><span class="content" style="font-size: 18px; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 1.5em; letter-spacing: 0em; text-align: left; font-weight: bold; display: block;">最核心的文章：《中国革命战争的战略问题》（1936年12月）</span><span class="suffix" style="display: none;"></span></h4>
<p data-tool="mdnice编辑器" style="color: rgb(74, 74, 74); font-size: 16px; line-height: 1.8em; letter-spacing: 0.02em; text-align: left; text-indent: 0em; margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; padding-top: 20px; padding-bottom: 8px; padding-left: 0px; padding-right: 0px;"><strong style="color: rgb(0, 0, 0); font-weight: bold; background-attachment: scroll; background-clip: border-box; background-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0); background-image: none; background-origin: padding-box; background-position-x: left; background-position-y: top; background-repeat: no-repeat; background-size: auto; width: auto; height: auto; margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; padding-top: 0px; padding-bottom: 0px; padding-left: 0px; padding-right: 0px; border-top-style: none; border-bottom-style: none; border-left-style: none; border-right-style: none; border-top-width: 3px; border-bottom-width: 3px; border-left-width: 3px; border-right-width: 3px; border-top-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.4); border-bottom-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.4); border-left-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.4); border-right-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.4); border-top-left-radius: 0px; border-top-right-radius: 0px; border-bottom-right-radius: 0px; border-bottom-left-radius: 0px;">核心思想</strong>：</p>
<blockquote class="custom-blockquote multiquote-1" data-tool="mdnice编辑器" style="margin-top: 20px; margin-bottom: 20px; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; padding-top: 10px; padding-bottom: 10px; padding-left: 20px; padding-right: 10px; border-top-style: none; border-bottom-style: none; border-left-style: none; border-right-style: none; border-top-width: 3px; border-bottom-width: 3px; border-left-width: 3px; border-right-width: 3px; border-top-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.4); border-bottom-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.4); border-left-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.4); border-right-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.4); border-top-left-radius: 0px; border-top-right-radius: 0px; border-bottom-right-radius: 0px; border-bottom-left-radius: 0px; background-attachment: scroll; background-clip: border-box; background-color: rgb(239, 239, 239); background-image: none; background-origin: padding-box; background-position-x: left; background-position-y: top; background-repeat: no-repeat; background-size: auto; width: auto; height: auto; box-shadow: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0) 0px 0px 0px 0px; display: block; overflow-x: auto; overflow-y: auto;"><span style="display: none; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); font-size: 16px; line-height: 1.5em; letter-spacing: 0em; text-align: left; font-weight: normal;"></span>
<p style="text-indent: 0em; padding-top: 20px; padding-bottom: 8px; padding-left: 0px; padding-right: 0px; color: rgb(89, 89, 89); font-size: 16px; line-height: 1.8em; letter-spacing: 0em; text-align: left; font-weight: normal; margin-top: 0px; margin-right: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; margin-left: 0px;">"战争的规律——这是任何指导战争的人不能不研究和不能不解决的问题。"<br>
"中国革命战争的规律，这是任何指导中国革命战争的人不能不研究和不能不解决的问题。"</p>
</blockquote>
<p data-tool="mdnice编辑器" style="color: rgb(74, 74, 74); font-size: 16px; line-height: 1.8em; letter-spacing: 0.02em; text-align: left; text-indent: 0em; margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; padding-top: 20px; padding-bottom: 8px; padding-left: 0px; padding-right: 0px;"><strong style="color: rgb(0, 0, 0); font-weight: bold; background-attachment: scroll; background-clip: border-box; background-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0); background-image: none; background-origin: padding-box; background-position-x: left; background-position-y: top; background-repeat: no-repeat; background-size: auto; width: auto; height: auto; margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; padding-top: 0px; padding-bottom: 0px; padding-left: 0px; padding-right: 0px; border-top-style: none; border-bottom-style: none; border-left-style: none; border-right-style: none; border-top-width: 3px; border-bottom-width: 3px; border-left-width: 3px; border-right-width: 3px; border-top-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.4); border-bottom-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.4); border-left-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.4); border-right-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.4); border-top-left-radius: 0px; border-top-right-radius: 0px; border-bottom-right-radius: 0px; border-bottom-left-radius: 0px;">为什么重要</strong>：
这篇文章系统论述了"方法从哪里来"：</p>
<ul data-tool="mdnice编辑器" style="list-style-type: disc; margin-top: 8px; margin-bottom: 8px; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; padding-top: 0px; padding-bottom: 0px; padding-left: 25px; padding-right: 0px; color: rgb(0, 0, 0);">
<li><section style="margin-top: 5px; margin-bottom: 5px; color: rgb(1, 1, 1); font-size: 16px; line-height: 1.8em; letter-spacing: 0em; text-align: left; font-weight: normal;">不是照搬苏联的经验（教条主义）</section></li><li><section style="margin-top: 5px; margin-bottom: 5px; color: rgb(1, 1, 1); font-size: 16px; line-height: 1.8em; letter-spacing: 0em; text-align: left; font-weight: normal;">不是照搬中国古代的兵法（复古主义）</section></li><li><section style="margin-top: 5px; margin-bottom: 5px; color: rgb(1, 1, 1); font-size: 16px; line-height: 1.8em; letter-spacing: 0em; text-align: left; font-weight: normal;">而是从"中国革命战争的特殊性"中总结出来</section></li></ul>
<p data-tool="mdnice编辑器" style="color: rgb(74, 74, 74); font-size: 16px; line-height: 1.8em; letter-spacing: 0.02em; text-align: left; text-indent: 0em; margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; padding-top: 20px; padding-bottom: 8px; padding-left: 0px; padding-right: 0px;"><strong style="color: rgb(0, 0, 0); font-weight: bold; background-attachment: scroll; background-clip: border-box; background-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0); background-image: none; background-origin: padding-box; background-position-x: left; background-position-y: top; background-repeat: no-repeat; background-size: auto; width: auto; height: auto; margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; padding-top: 0px; padding-bottom: 0px; padding-left: 0px; padding-right: 0px; border-top-style: none; border-bottom-style: none; border-left-style: none; border-right-style: none; border-top-width: 3px; border-bottom-width: 3px; border-left-width: 3px; border-right-width: 3px; border-top-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.4); border-bottom-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.4); border-left-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.4); border-right-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.4); border-top-left-radius: 0px; border-top-right-radius: 0px; border-bottom-right-radius: 0px; border-bottom-left-radius: 0px;">提出了著名的战术原则</strong>：</p>
<ul data-tool="mdnice编辑器" style="list-style-type: disc; margin-top: 8px; margin-bottom: 8px; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; padding-top: 0px; padding-bottom: 0px; padding-left: 25px; padding-right: 0px; color: rgb(0, 0, 0);">
<li><section style="margin-top: 5px; margin-bottom: 5px; color: rgb(1, 1, 1); font-size: 16px; line-height: 1.8em; letter-spacing: 0em; text-align: left; font-weight: normal;">"十六字诀"：敌进我退，敌驻我扰，敌疲我打，敌退我追</section></li><li><section style="margin-top: 5px; margin-bottom: 5px; color: rgb(1, 1, 1); font-size: 16px; line-height: 1.8em; letter-spacing: 0em; text-align: left; font-weight: normal;">"诱敌深入"</section></li><li><section style="margin-top: 5px; margin-bottom: 5px; color: rgb(1, 1, 1); font-size: 16px; line-height: 1.8em; letter-spacing: 0em; text-align: left; font-weight: normal;">"集中优势兵力，各个歼灭敌人"</section></li></ul>
<p data-tool="mdnice编辑器" style="color: rgb(74, 74, 74); font-size: 16px; line-height: 1.8em; letter-spacing: 0.02em; text-align: left; text-indent: 0em; margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; padding-top: 20px; padding-bottom: 8px; padding-left: 0px; padding-right: 0px;"><strong style="color: rgb(0, 0, 0); font-weight: bold; background-attachment: scroll; background-clip: border-box; background-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0); background-image: none; background-origin: padding-box; background-position-x: left; background-position-y: top; background-repeat: no-repeat; background-size: auto; width: auto; height: auto; margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; padding-top: 0px; padding-bottom: 0px; padding-left: 0px; padding-right: 0px; border-top-style: none; border-bottom-style: none; border-left-style: none; border-right-style: none; border-top-width: 3px; border-bottom-width: 3px; border-left-width: 3px; border-right-width: 3px; border-top-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.4); border-bottom-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.4); border-left-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.4); border-right-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.4); border-top-left-radius: 0px; border-top-right-radius: 0px; border-bottom-right-radius: 0px; border-bottom-left-radius: 0px;">对应九字真言</strong>：
这些方法不是拍脑袋想出来的，而是基于对"敌强我弱"这个基本情况的认识，从实践中总结出来的。</p>
<hr data-tool="mdnice编辑器" style="margin-top: 10px; margin-bottom: 10px; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; padding-top: 0px; padding-bottom: 0px; padding-left: 0px; padding-right: 0px; border-top-style: none; border-bottom-style: none; border-left-style: none; border-right-style: none; border-top-width: 1px; border-bottom-width: 3px; border-left-width: 3px; border-right-width: 3px; border-top-color: rgb(0, 0, 0); border-bottom-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.4); border-left-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.4); border-right-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.4); border-top-left-radius: 0px; border-top-right-radius: 0px; border-bottom-right-radius: 0px; border-bottom-left-radius: 0px; background-attachment: scroll; background-clip: border-box; background-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0); background-image: linear-gradient(90deg, rgba(60, 112, 198, 0) 0%, rgba(60, 122, 198, 0.75) 50%, rgba(60, 122, 198, 0) 100%); background-origin: padding-box; background-position-x: left; background-position-y: top; background-repeat: no-repeat; background-size: auto; width: auto; height: 1px;">
<h4 data-tool="mdnice编辑器" style="margin-top: 30px; margin-bottom: 15px; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; padding-top: 0px; padding-bottom: 0px; padding-left: 0px; padding-right: 0px; display: block;"><span class="prefix" style="display: none;"></span><span class="content" style="font-size: 18px; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 1.5em; letter-spacing: 0em; text-align: left; font-weight: bold; display: block;">第二重要：《论十大关系》（1956年4月）</span><span class="suffix" style="display: none;"></span></h4>
<p data-tool="mdnice编辑器" style="color: rgb(74, 74, 74); font-size: 16px; line-height: 1.8em; letter-spacing: 0.02em; text-align: left; text-indent: 0em; margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; padding-top: 20px; padding-bottom: 8px; padding-left: 0px; padding-right: 0px;"><strong style="color: rgb(0, 0, 0); font-weight: bold; background-attachment: scroll; background-clip: border-box; background-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0); background-image: none; background-origin: padding-box; background-position-x: left; background-position-y: top; background-repeat: no-repeat; background-size: auto; width: auto; height: auto; margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; padding-top: 0px; padding-bottom: 0px; padding-left: 0px; padding-right: 0px; border-top-style: none; border-bottom-style: none; border-left-style: none; border-right-style: none; border-top-width: 3px; border-bottom-width: 3px; border-left-width: 3px; border-right-width: 3px; border-top-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.4); border-bottom-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.4); border-left-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.4); border-right-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.4); border-top-left-radius: 0px; border-top-right-radius: 0px; border-bottom-right-radius: 0px; border-bottom-left-radius: 0px;">核心思想</strong>：</p>
<blockquote class="custom-blockquote multiquote-1" data-tool="mdnice编辑器" style="margin-top: 20px; margin-bottom: 20px; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; padding-top: 10px; padding-bottom: 10px; padding-left: 20px; padding-right: 10px; border-top-style: none; border-bottom-style: none; border-left-style: none; border-right-style: none; border-top-width: 3px; border-bottom-width: 3px; border-left-width: 3px; border-right-width: 3px; border-top-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.4); border-bottom-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.4); border-left-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.4); border-right-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.4); border-top-left-radius: 0px; border-top-right-radius: 0px; border-bottom-right-radius: 0px; border-bottom-left-radius: 0px; background-attachment: scroll; background-clip: border-box; background-color: rgb(239, 239, 239); background-image: none; background-origin: padding-box; background-position-x: left; background-position-y: top; background-repeat: no-repeat; background-size: auto; width: auto; height: auto; box-shadow: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0) 0px 0px 0px 0px; display: block; overflow-x: auto; overflow-y: auto;"><span style="display: none; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); font-size: 16px; line-height: 1.5em; letter-spacing: 0em; text-align: left; font-weight: normal;"></span>
<p style="text-indent: 0em; padding-top: 20px; padding-bottom: 8px; padding-left: 0px; padding-right: 0px; color: rgb(89, 89, 89); font-size: 16px; line-height: 1.8em; letter-spacing: 0em; text-align: left; font-weight: normal; margin-top: 0px; margin-right: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; margin-left: 0px;">"最近苏联方面暴露了他们在建设社会主义过程中的一些缺点和错误，他们走过的弯路，你还想走？过去我们就是鉴于他们的经验教训，少走了一些弯路，现在当然更要引以为戒。"</p>
</blockquote>
