<p data-tool="mdnice编辑器" style="color: rgb(74, 74, 74); font-size: 16px; line-height: 1.8em; letter-spacing: 0.02em; text-align: left; text-indent: 0em; margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; padding-top: 20px; padding-bottom: 8px; padding-left: 0px; padding-right: 0px;"><strong style="color: rgb(0, 0, 0); font-weight: bold; background-attachment: scroll; background-clip: border-box; background-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0); background-image: none; background-origin: padding-box; background-position-x: left; background-position-y: top; background-repeat: no-repeat; background-size: auto; width: auto; height: auto; margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; padding-top: 0px; padding-bottom: 0px; padding-left: 0px; padding-right: 0px; border-top-style: none; border-bottom-style: none; border-left-style: none; border-right-style: none; border-top-width: 3px; border-bottom-width: 3px; border-left-width: 3px; border-right-width: 3px; border-top-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.4); border-bottom-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.4); border-left-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.4); border-right-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.4); border-top-left-radius: 0px; border-top-right-radius: 0px; border-bottom-right-radius: 0px; border-bottom-left-radius: 0px;">为什么重要</strong>：
这篇讲话体现了"方法对"的核心原则：</p>
<ul data-tool="mdnice编辑器" style="list-style-type: disc; margin-top: 8px; margin-bottom: 8px; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; padding-top: 0px; padding-bottom: 0px; padding-left: 25px; padding-right: 0px; color: rgb(0, 0, 0);">
<li><section style="margin-top: 5px; margin-bottom: 5px; color: rgb(1, 1, 1); font-size: 16px; line-height: 1.8em; letter-spacing: 0em; text-align: left; font-weight: normal;">不照搬别人的经验（哪怕是苏联老大哥）</section></li><li><section style="margin-top: 5px; margin-bottom: 5px; color: rgb(1, 1, 1); font-size: 16px; line-height: 1.8em; letter-spacing: 0em; text-align: left; font-weight: normal;">从中国的实际情况出发</section></li><li><section style="margin-top: 5px; margin-bottom: 5px; color: rgb(1, 1, 1); font-size: 16px; line-height: 1.8em; letter-spacing: 0em; text-align: left; font-weight: normal;">"以苏为鉴"，走自己的路</section></li></ul>
<hr data-tool="mdnice编辑器" style="margin-top: 10px; margin-bottom: 10px; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; padding-top: 0px; padding-bottom: 0px; padding-left: 0px; padding-right: 0px; border-top-style: none; border-bottom-style: none; border-left-style: none; border-right-style: none; border-top-width: 1px; border-bottom-width: 3px; border-left-width: 3px; border-right-width: 3px; border-top-color: rgb(0, 0, 0); border-bottom-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.4); border-left-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.4); border-right-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.4); border-top-left-radius: 0px; border-top-right-radius: 0px; border-bottom-right-radius: 0px; border-bottom-left-radius: 0px; background-attachment: scroll; background-clip: border-box; background-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0); background-image: linear-gradient(90deg, rgba(60, 112, 198, 0) 0%, rgba(60, 122, 198, 0.75) 50%, rgba(60, 122, 198, 0) 100%); background-origin: padding-box; background-position-x: left; background-position-y: top; background-repeat: no-repeat; background-size: auto; width: auto; height: 1px;">
<h2 data-tool="mdnice编辑器" style="margin-top: 30px; margin-bottom: 15px; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; padding-left: 0px; padding-right: 0px; border-top-style: none; background-attachment: scroll; background-clip: border-box; background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255); background-image: url('https://files.mdnice.com/mountain_2.png'); background-origin: padding-box; background-position-x: center; background-position-y: center; background-repeat: no-repeat; background-size: 63px; width: auto; height: auto; align-items: unset; border-bottom-style: none; border-left-style: none; border-right-style: none; border-top-width: 1px; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-left-width: 1px; border-right-width: 1px; border-top-color: rgb(0, 0, 0); border-bottom-color: rgb(0, 0, 0); border-left-color: rgb(0, 0, 0); border-right-color: rgb(0, 0, 0); border-top-left-radius: 0px; border-top-right-radius: 0px; border-bottom-left-radius: 0px; border-bottom-right-radius: 0px; box-shadow: none; display: flex; flex-direction: unset; float: unset; justify-content: center; line-height: 1.5em; overflow-x: unset; overflow-y: unset; padding-top: 0px; padding-bottom: 0px; position: relative; text-align: left; text-shadow: none; transform: none; -webkit-box-reflect: unset;"><span class="prefix" style="display: none;"></span><span class="content" style="font-size: 18px; color: rgb(60, 112, 198); line-height: 2.4em; letter-spacing: 0em; margin-top: 38px; margin-bottom: 10px; border-bottom-style: none; border-left-style: none; border-right-style: none; border-top-width: 1px; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-left-width: 1px; border-right-width: 1px; border-top-color: rgb(0, 0, 0); border-bottom-color: rgb(0, 0, 0); border-left-color: rgb(0, 0, 0); border-right-color: rgb(0, 0, 0); <p data-tool="mdnice编辑器" style="color: rgb(74, 74, 74); font-size: 16px; line-height: 1.8em; letter-spacing: 0.02em; text-align: left; text-indent: 0em; margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; padding-top: 20px; padding-bottom: 8px; padding-left: 0px; padding-right: 0px;">虽然"情况明、决心大、方法对"这九个字是1961年才说的，但这套思想在《毛选》里一以贯之：</p>

<h2 data-tool="mdnice编辑器" style="margin-top: 30px; margin-bottom: 15px; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; padding-left: 0px; padding-right: 0px; border-top-style: none; background-attachment: scroll; background-clip: border-box; background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255); background-image: url('https://files.mdnice.com/mountain_2.png'); background-origin: padding-box; background-position-x: center; background-position-y: center; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-left-width: 1px; border-right-width: 1px; border-top-color: rgb(0, 0, 0); border-bottom-color: rgb(0, 0, 0); border-left-color: rgb(0, 0, 0); border-right-color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 1.5em; overflow-x: unset; overflow-y: unset; padding-top: 0px; padding-bottom: 0px; position: relative; text-align: left; text-shadow: none; transform: none; -webkit-box-reflect: unset;"><span class="prefix" style="display: none;"></span><span class="content" style="font-size: 18px; color: rgb(60, 112, 198); line-height: 2.4em; letter-spacing: 0em; margin-top: 38px; margin-bottom: 10px; border-bottom-style: none; border-left-style: none; border-right-style: none; border-top-width: 1px; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-left-width: 1px; border-right-width: 1px; border-top-color: rgb(0, 0, 0); border-bottom-color: rgb(0, 0, 0); border-left-color: rgb(0, 0, 0); border-right-color: rgb(0, 0, 0); border-top-left-radius: 0px; border-top-right-radius: 0px; border-bottom-left-radius: 0px; border-bottom-right-radius: 0px; align-items: unset; background-attachment: scroll; background-clip: border-box; box-shadow: none; display: inline-block; font-weight: bold; flex-direction: unset; float: unset; height: 38px; justify-content: unset; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; overflow-x: unset; overflow-y: unset; padding-top: 0px; padding-bottom: 0px; padding-left: 0px; padding-right: 0px; position: relative; text-align: center; text-indent: 0em; text-shadow: none; transform: none; width: auto; -webkit-box-reflect: unset;">四、为什么1961年才提出这九个字？</span><span class="suffix" style="display: none;"></span></h2>
<p data-tool="mdnice编辑器" style="color: rgb(74, 74, 74); font-size: 16px; line-height: 1.8em; letter-spacing: 0.02em; text-align: left; text-indent: 0em; margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; padding-top: 20px; padding-bottom: 8px; padding-left: 0px; padding-right: 0px;">因为到了1961年，毛泽东需要总结"大跃进"的教训。</p>
<p data-tool="mdnice编辑器" style="color: rgb(74, 74, 74); font-size: 16px; line-height: 1.8em; letter-spacing: 0.02em; text-align: left; text-indent: 0em; margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; padding-top: 20px; padding-bottom: 8px; padding-left: 0px; padding-right: 0px;"><strong style="color: rgb(0, 0, 0); font-weight: bold; background-attachment: scroll; background-clip: border-box; background-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0); background-image: none; background-origin: padding-box; background-position-x: left; background-position-y: top; background-repeat: no-repeat; background-size: auto; width: auto; height: auto; margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; padding-top: 0px; padding-bottom: 0px; padding-left: 0px; padding-right: 0px; border-top-style: none; border-bottom-style: none; border-left-style: none; border-right-style: none; border-top-width: 3px; border-bottom-width: 3px; border-left-width: 3px; border-right-width: 3px; border-top-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.4); border-bottom-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.4); border-left-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.4); border-right-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.4); border-top-left-radius: 0px; border-top-right-radius: 0px; border-bottom-right-radius: 0px; border-bottom-left-radius: 0px;">大跃进的错误，正是违反了这九个字</strong>：</p>
<ul data-tool="mdnice编辑器" style="list-style-type: disc; margin-top: 8px; margin-bottom: 8px; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; padding-top: 0px; padding-bottom: 0px; padding-left: 25px; padding-right: 0px; color: rgb(0, 0, 0);">
<li><section style="margin-top: 5px; margin-bottom: 5px; color: rgb(1, 1, 1); font-size: 16px; line-height: 1.8em; letter-spacing: 0em; text-align: left; font-weight: normal;"><strong style="color: rgb(0, 0, 0); font-weight: bold; background-attachment: scroll; background-clip: border-box; background-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0); background-image: none; background-origin: padding-box; background-position-x: left; background-position-y: top; background-repeat: no-repeat; background-size: auto; width: auto; height: auto; margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; padding-top: 0px; padding-bottom: 0px; padding-left: 0px; padding-right: 0px; border-top-style: none; border-bottom-style: none; border-left-style: none; border-right-style: none; border-top-width: 3px; border-bottom-width: 3px; border-left-width: 3px; border-right-width: 3px; border-top-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.4); border-bottom-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.4); border-left-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.4); border-right-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.4); border-top-left-radius: 0px; border-top-right-radius: 0px; border-bottom-right-radius: 0px; border-bottom-left-radius: 0px;">情况不明</strong>：对中国的生产力水平、资源状况缺乏深入调查，盲目提出"超英赶美"</section></li><li><section style="margin-top: 5px; margin-bottom: 5px; color: rgb(1, 1, 1); font-size: 16px; line-height: 1.8em; letter-spacing: 0em; text-align: left; font-weight: normal;"><strong style="color: rgb(0, 0, 0); font-weight: bold; background-attachment: scroll; background-clip: border-box; background-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0); background-image: none; background-origin: padding-box; background-position-x: left; background-position-y: top; background-repeat: no-repeat; background-size: auto; width: auto; height: auto; margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; padding-top: 0px; padding-bottom: 0px; padding-left: 0px; padding-right: 0px; border-top-style: none; border-bottom-style: none; border-left-style: none; border-right-style: none; border-top-width: 3px; border-bottom-width: 3px; border-left-width: 3px; border-right-width: 3px; border-top-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.4); border-bottom-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.4); border-left-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.4); border-right-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.4); border-top-left-radius: 0px; border-top-right-radius: 0px; border-bottom-right-radius: 0px; border-bottom-left-radius: 0px;">决心错位</strong>：决心很大，但建立在错误的情况判断上（高估了人的主观能动性）</section></li><li><section style="margin-top: 5px; margin-bottom: 5px; color: rgb(1, 1, 1); font-size: 16px; line-height: 1.8em; letter-spacing: 0em; text-align: left; font-weight: normal;"><strong style="color: rgb(0, 0, 0); font-weight: bold; background-attachment: scroll; background-clip: border-box; background-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0); background-image: none; background-origin: padding-box; background-position-x: left; background-position-y: top; background-repeat: no-repeat; background-size: auto; width: auto; height: auto; margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; padding-top: 0px; padding-bottom: 0px; padding-left: 0px; padding-right: 0px; border-top-style: none; border-bottom-style: none; border-left-style: none; border-right-style: none; border-top-width: 3px; border-bottom-width: 3px; border-left-width: 3px; border-right-width: 3px; border-top-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.4); border-bottom-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.4); border-left-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.4); border-right-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.4); border-top-left-radius: 0px; border-top-right-radius: 0px; border-bottom-right-radius: 0px; border-bottom-left-radius: 0px;">方法错误</strong>：用"大炼钢铁"、"亩产万斤"这种违背规律的方法</section></li></ul>
<p data-tool="mdnice编辑器" style="color: rgb(74, 74, 74); font-size: 16px; line-height: 1.8em; letter-spacing: 0.02em; text-align: left; text-indent: 0em; margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; padding-top: 20px; padding-bottom: 8px; padding-left: 0px; padding-right: 0px;">所以，1961年的这次讲话，本质上是一次<strong style="color: rgb(0, 0, 0); font-weight: bold; background-attachment: scroll; background-clip: border-box; background-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0); background-image: none; background-origin: padding-box; background-position-x: left; background-position-y: top; background-repeat: no-repeat; background-size: auto; width: auto; height: auto; margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; padding-top: 0px; padding-bottom: 0px; padding-left: 0px; padding-right: 0px; border-top-style: none; border-bottom-style: none; border-left-style: none; border-right-style: none; border-top-width: 3px; border-bottom-width: 3px; border-left-width: 3px; border-right-width: 3px; border-top-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.4); border-bottom-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.4); border-left-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.4); border-right-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.4); border-top-left-radius: 0px; border-top-right-radius: 0px; border-bottom-right-radius: 0px; border-bottom-left-radius: 0px;">痛定思痛的自我批评</strong>：</p>
<blockquote class="custom-blockquote multiquote-1" data-tool="mdnice编辑器" style="margin-top: 20px; margin-bottom: 20px; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; padding-top: 10px; padding-bottom: 10px; padding-left: 20px; padding-right: 10px; border-top-style: none; border-bottom-style: none; border-left-style: none; border-right-style: none; border-top-width: 3px; border-bottom-width: 3px; border-left-width: 3px; border-right-width: 3px; border-top-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.4); border-bottom-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.4); border-left-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.4); border-right-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.4); border-top-left-radius: 0px; border-top-right-radius: 0px; border-bottom-right-radius: 0px; border-bottom-left-radius: 0px; background-attachment: scroll; background-clip: border-box; background-color: rgb(239, 239, 239); background-image: none; background-origin: padding-box; background-position-x: left; background-position-y: top; background-repeat: no-repeat; background-size: auto; width: auto; height: auto; box-shadow: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0) 0px 0px 0px 0px; display: block; overflow-x: auto; overflow-y: auto;"><span style="display: none; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); font-size: 16px; line-height: 1.5em; letter-spacing: 0em; text-align: left; font-weight: normal;"></span>
<p style="text-indent: 0em; padding-top: 20px; padding-bottom: 8px; padding-left: 0px; padding-right: 0px; color: rgb(89, 89, 89); font-size: 16px; line-height: 1.8em; letter-spacing: 0em; text-align: left; font-weight: normal; margin-top: 0px; margin-right: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; margin-left: 0px;">"我们今后不能再犯这种错误了。要做到：情况明，决心大，方法对。"</p>
</blockquote>
<hr data-tool="mdnice编辑器" style="margin-top: 10px; margin-bottom: 10px; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; padding-top: 0px; padding-bottom: 0px; padding-left: 0px; padding-right: 0px; border-top-style: none; border-bottom-style: none; border-left-style: none; border-right-style: none; border-top-width: 1px; border-bottom-width: 3px; border-left-width: 3px; border-right-width: 3px; border-top-color: rgb(0, 0, 0); border-bottom-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.4); border-left-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.4); border-right-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.4); border-top-left-radius: 0px; border-top-right-radius: 0px; border-bottom-right-radius: 0px; border-bottom-left-radius: 0px; background-attachment: scroll; background-clip: border-box; background-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0); background-image: linear-gradient(90deg, rgba(60, 112, 198, 0) 0%, rgba(60, 122, 198, 0.75) 50%, rgba(60, 122, 198, 0) 100%); background-origin: padding-box; background-position-x: left; background-position-y: top; background-repeat: no-repeat; background-size: auto; width: auto; height: 1px;">
</section>

<section id="nice" data-tool="mdnice编辑器" data-website="https://www.mdnice.com" style="margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; padding-top: 0px; padding-bottom: 0px; padding-left: 10px; padding-left: 0px; padding-right: 0px; position: relative; text-align: center; text-indent: 0em; text-shadow: none; transform: none; width: auto; -webkit-box-reflect: unset;">Clear Situation, Great Resolve, Correct Method</span><span class="suffix" style="display: none;"></span></h1>
<h2 data-tool="mdnice编辑器" style="margin-top: 30px; margin-bottom: 15px; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; padding-left: 0px; padding-right: 0px; border-top-style: none; background-attachment: scroll; Source</span><span class="suffix" style="display: none;"></span></h2>
<p data-tool="mdnice编辑器" style="color: rgb(74, 74, 74); font-size: 16px; line-height: 1.8em; letter-spacing: 0.02em; text-align: left; text-indent: 0em; margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; padding-top: 20px; padding-bottom: 8px; padding-left: 0px; padding-right: 0px;"><strong style="color: rgb(0, 0, 0); font-weight: bold; background-attachment: scroll; background-clip: border-box; background-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0); background-image: none; background-origin: padding-box; background-position-x: left; background-position-y: top; background-repeat: no-repeat; background-size: auto; width: auto; height: auto; margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; padding-top: 0px; padding-bottom: 0px; padding-left: 0px; padding-right: 0px; border-top-style: none; border-bottom-style: none; border-left-style: none; border-right-style: none; border-top-width: 3px; border-bottom-width: 3px; border-left-width: 3px; border-right-width: 3px; border-top-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.4); border-bottom-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.4); border-left-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.4); border-right-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.4); border-top-left-radius: 0px; border-top-right-radius: 0px; border-bottom-right-radius: 0px; border-bottom-left-radius: 0px;">The nine characters "Clear Situation, Great Resolve, Correct Method" (情况明、决心大、方法对) do not appear in any single article of the <em style="color: rgb(0, 0, 0); font-weight: bold; font-style: italic; background-attachment: scroll; background-clip: border-box; background-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0); background-image: none; background-origin: padding-box; background-position-x: left; background-position-y: top; background-repeat: no-repeat; background-size: auto; width: auto; height: auto; margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; padding-top: 0px; padding-bottom: 0px; padding-left: 0px; padding-right: 0px; border-top-style: none; border-bottom-style: none; border-left-style: none; border-right-style: none; border-top-width: 3px; border-bottom-width: 3px; border-left-width: 3px; border-right-width: 3px; border-top-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.4); border-bottom-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.4); border-left-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.4); border-right-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.4); border-top-left-radius: 0px; border-top-right-radius: 0px; border-bottom-right-radius: 0px; border-bottom-left-radius: 0px;">Selected Works</em>. Instead, they were spoken by Mao Zedong at a Central Work Conference in January 1961.</strong></p>
<p data-tool="mdnice编辑器" style="color: rgb(74, 74, 74); font-size: 16px; line-height: 1.8em; letter-spacing: 0.02em; text-align: left; text-indent: 0em; margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; padding-top: 20px; padding-bottom: 8px; padding-left: 0px; padding-right: 0px;">Context:</p>
<ul data-tool="mdnice编辑器" style="list-style-type: disc; margin-top: 8px; margin-bottom: 8px; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; padding-top: 0px; padding-bottom: 0px; padding-left: 25px; padding-right: 0px; color: rgb(0, 0, 0);">
<li><section style="margin-top: 5px; margin-bottom: 5px; color: rgb(1, 1, 1); font-size: 16px; line-height: 1.8em; letter-spacing: 0em; text-align: left; font-weight: normal;"><strong style="color: rgb(0, 0, 0); font-weight: bold; background-attachment: scroll; background-clip: border-box; background-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0); background-image: none; background-origin: padding-box; background-position-x: left; background-position-y: top; background-repeat: no-repeat; background-size: auto; width: auto; height: auto; margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; padding-top: 0px; padding-bottom: 0px; padding-left: 0px; padding-right: 0px; border-top-style: none; border-bottom-style: none; border-left-style: none; border-right-style: none; border-top-width: 3px; border-bottom-width: 3px; border-left-width: 3px; border-right-width: 3px; border-top-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.4); border-bottom-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.4); border-left-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.4); border-right-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.4); border-top-left-radius: 0px; border-top-right-radius: 0px; border-bottom-right-radius: 0px; border-bottom-left-radius: 0px;">Time</strong>: January 1961</section></li><li><section style="margin-top: 5px; margin-bottom: 5px; color: rgb(1, 1, 1); font-size: 16px; line-height: 1.8em; letter-spacing: 0em; text-align: left; font-weight: normal;"><strong style="color: rgb(0, 0, 0); font-weight: bold; background-attachment: scroll; background-clip: border-box; background-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0); background-image: none; background-origin: padding-box; background-position-x: left; background-position-y: top; background-repeat: no-repeat; background-size: auto; width: auto; height: auto; margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; padding-top: 0px; padding-bottom: 0px; padding-left: 0px; padding-right: 0px; border-top-style: none; border-bottom-style: none; border-left-style: none; border-right-style: none; border-top-width: 3px; border-bottom-width: 3px; border-left-width: 3px; border-right-width: 3px; border-top-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.4); border-bottom-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.4); border-left-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.4); border-right-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.4); border-top-left-radius: 0px; border-top-right-radius: 0px; border-bottom-right-radius: 0px; border-bottom-left-radius: 0px;">Occasion</strong>: Central Work Conference (also known as the preparatory meeting for the "Seven Thousand Cadres Conference")</section></li><li><section style="margin-top: 5px; margin-bottom: 5px; color: rgb(1, 1, 1); font-size: 16px; line-height: 1.8em; letter-spacing: 0em; text-align: left; font-weight: normal;"><strong style="color: rgb(0, 0, 0); font-weight: bold; background-attachment: scroll; background-clip: border-box; background-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0); background-image: none; background-origin: padding-box; background-position-x: left; background-position-y: top; background-repeat: no-repeat; background-size: auto; width: auto; height: auto; margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; padding-top: 0px; padding-bottom: 0px; padding-left: 0px; padding-right: 0px; border-top-style: none; border-bottom-style: none; border-left-style: none; border-right-style: none; border-top-width: 3px; border-bottom-width: 3px; border-left-width: 3px; border-right-width: 3px; border-top-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.4); border-bottom-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.4); border-left-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.4); border-right-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.4); border-top-left-radius: 0px; border-top-right-radius: 0px; border-bottom-right-radius: 0px; border-bottom-left-radius: 0px;">Background</strong>: During the period of severe national economic difficulties caused by the consequences of the "Great Leap Forward."</section></li><li><section style="margin-top: 5px; margin-bottom: 5px; color: rgb(1, 1, 1); font-size: 16px; line-height: 1.8em; letter-spacing: 0em; text-align: left; font-weight: normal;"><strong style="color: rgb(0, 0, 0); font-weight: bold; background-attachment: scroll; border-top-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.4); border-bottom-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.4); border-left-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.4); border-right-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.4); border-top-left-radius: 0px; border-top-right-radius: 0px; border-bottom-right-radius: 0px; border-bottom-left-radius: 0px;">Original Quote</strong>:</section></li></ul>
<blockquote class="custom-blockquote multiquote-1" data-tool="mdnice编辑器" style="margin-top: 20px; margin-bottom: 20px; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; padding-top: 10px; padding-bottom: 10px; padding-left: 20px; padding-right: 10px; border-top-style: none; border-bottom-style: none; border-left-style: none; border-right-style: none; border-top-width: 3px; border-bottom-width: 3px; border-left-width: 3px; border-right-width: 3px; border-top-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.4); border-bottom-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.4); border-left-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.4); border-right-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.4); border-top-left-radius: 0px; border-top-right-radius: 0px; border-bottom-right-radius: 0px; border-bottom-left-radius: 0px; background-attachment: scroll; background-clip: border-box; background-color: rgb(239, 239, 239); background-image: none; background-origin: padding-box; background-position-x: left; background-position-y: top; background-repeat: no-repeat; background-size: auto; width: auto; height: auto; box-shadow: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0) 0px 0px 0px 0px; display: block; overflow-x: auto; overflow-y: auto;"><span style="display: none; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); font-size: 16px; line-height: 1.5em; letter-spacing: 0em; text-align: left; font-weight: normal;"></span>
<p style="text-indent: 0em; padding-top: 20px; padding-bottom: 8px; padding-left: 0px; padding-right: 0px; color: rgb(89, 89, 89); font-size: 16px; line-height: 1.8em; letter-spacing: 0em; text-align: left; font-weight: normal; margin-top: 0px; margin-right: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; margin-left: 0px;">"In our future work, we must achieve three things: clear situation, great resolve, and correct method."</p>
</blockquote>
<p data-tool="mdnice编辑器" style="color: rgb(74, 74, 74); font-size: 16px; line-height: 1.8em; letter-spacing: 0.02em; text-align: left; text-indent: 0em; margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; padding-top: 20px; padding-bottom: 8px; padding-left: 0px; padding-right: 0px;">This statement was later included in:</p>
<ul data-tool="mdnice编辑器" style="list-style-type: disc; margin-top: 8px; margin-bottom: 8px; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; padding-top: 0px; padding-bottom: 0px; padding-left: 25px; padding-right: 0px; color: rgb(0, 0, 0);">
<li><section style="margin-top: 5px; margin-bottom: 5px; color: rgb(1, 1, 1); font-size: 16px; line-height: 1.8em; letter-spacing: 0em; text-align: left; font-weight: normal;"><em style="color: rgb(0, 0, 0); <p data-tool="mdnice编辑器" style="color: rgb(74, 74, 74); font-size: 16px; line-height: 1.8em; letter-spacing: 0.02em; text-align: left; text-indent: 0em; margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; padding-top: 20px; padding-bottom: 8px; padding-left: 0px; padding-right: 0px;"><strong style="color: rgb(0, 0, 0); font-weight: bold; background-attachment: scroll; background-clip: border-box; border-bottom-left-radius: 0px;">However</strong>, although these nine characters were explicitly formulated in 1961, this system of thought permeates the entirety of the <em style="color: rgb(0, 0, 0); font-style: italic; background-attachment: scroll; background-clip: border-box; background-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0); background-image: none; background-origin: padding-box; background-position-x: left; <hr data-tool="mdnice编辑器" style="margin-top: 10px; margin-bottom: 10px; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; padding-top: 0px; padding-bottom: 0px; padding-left: 0px; padding-right: 0px; border-top-style: none; border-bottom-style: none; border-left-style: none; border-right-style: none; border-top-width: 1px; border-bottom-width: 3px; border-left-width: 3px; border-right-width: 3px; border-top-color: rgb(0, 0, 0); border-bottom-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.4); border-left-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.4); border-right-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.4); border-top-left-radius: 0px; border-top-right-radius: 0px; border-bottom-right-radius: 0px; border-bottom-left-radius: 0px; background-attachment: scroll; background-clip: border-box; background-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0); background-image: linear-gradient(90deg, rgba(60, 112, 198, 0) 0%, rgba(60, 122, 198, 0.75) 50%, rgba(60, 122, 198, 0) 100%); background-origin: padding-box; background-position-x: left; background-position-y: top; background-repeat: no-repeat; background-size: auto; width: auto; height: 1px;">

Core Articles in the <em style="color: rgb(0, 0, 0); font-style: italic; background-attachment: scroll; background-clip: border-box; background-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0); background-image: none; background-origin: padding-box; background-position-x: left; background-position-y: top; background-repeat: no-repeat; background-size: auto; width: auto; height: auto; margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; padding-top: 0px; padding-bottom: 0px; padding-left: 0px; padding-right: 0px; border-top-style: none; border-bottom-style: none; border-left-style: none; border-right-style: none; border-top-width: 3px; border-bottom-width: 3px; border-left-width: 3px; border-right-width: 3px; border-top-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.4); border-bottom-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.4); border-left-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.4); border-right-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.4); border-top-left-radius: 0px; border-top-right-radius: 0px; border-bottom-right-radius: 0px; border-bottom-left-radius: 0px;">Selected Works</em> Reflecting This Thought</span><span class="suffix" style="display: none;"></span></h2>
<p data-tool="mdnice编辑器" style="color: rgb(74, 74, 74); font-size: 16px; line-height: 1.8em; letter-spacing: 0.02em; text-align: left; text-indent: 0em; margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; padding-top: 20px; padding-bottom: 8px; padding-left: 0px; padding-right: 0px;">While <strong style="color: rgb(0, 0, 0); font-weight: bold; background-attachment: scroll; background-clip: border-box; background-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0); background-image: none; background-origin: padding-box; background-position-x: left; background-position-y: top; background-repeat: no-repeat; background-size: auto; width: auto; height: auto; margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; padding-top: 0px; padding-bottom: 0px; padding-left: 0px; padding-right: 0px; border-top-style: none; border-bottom-style: none; border-left-style: none; border-right-style: none; border-top-width: 3px; border-bottom-width: 3px; border-left-width: 3px; border-right-width: 3px; border-top-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.4); border-bottom-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.4); border-left-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.4); border-right-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.4); border-top-left-radius: 0px; border-top-right-radius: 0px; border-bottom-right-radius: 0px; border-bottom-left-radius: 0px;">Clear Situation, Great Resolve, Correct Method</strong> appeared late as a complete phrase, its intellectual roots can be traced back to several classic articles in the <em style="color: rgb(0, 0, 0); padding-bottom: 0px; padding-left: 0px; padding-right: 0px; border-top-style: none; border-bottom-style: none; border-left-style: none; border-right-style: none; border-top-width: 3px; border-bottom-width: 3px; border-left-width: 3px; border-right-width: 3px; border-top-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.4); border-bottom-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.4); border-left-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.4); border-right-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.4); border-top-left-radius: 0px; border-top-right-radius: 0px; border-bottom-right-radius: 0px; border-bottom-left-radius: 0px;">Selected Works</em>:</p>
<h3 data-tool="mdnice编辑器" style="margin-top: 30px; margin-bottom: 15px; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; padding-top: 0px; padding-bottom: 0px; padding-left: 0px; padding-right: 0px; align-items: unset; The Intellectual Source of [Clear Situation]</span><span class="suffix" style="display: none;"></span></h3>
<h4 data-tool="mdnice编辑器" style="margin-top: 30px; margin-bottom: 15px; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; padding-top: 0px; padding-bottom: 0px; padding-left: 0px; padding-right: 0px; display: block;"><span class="prefix" style="display: none;"></span><span class="content" style="font-size: 18px; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 1.5em; letter-spacing: 0em; text-align: left; font-weight: bold; display: block;">The Most Core Article: <em style="color: rgb(0, 0, 0); font-style: italic; background-attachment: scroll; background-clip: border-box; background-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0); background-image: none; background-origin: padding-box; background-position-x: left; background-position-y: top; background-repeat: no-repeat; background-size: auto; width: auto; height: auto; margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; padding-top: 0px; padding-bottom: 0px; padding-left: 0px; padding-right: 0px; border-top-style: none; border-bottom-style: none; border-left-style: none; border-right-style: none; border-top-width: 3px; border-bottom-width: 3px; border-left-width: 3px; border-right-width: 3px; border-top-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.4); border-bottom-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.4); border-left-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.4); border-right-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.4); border-top-left-radius: 0px; border-top-right-radius: 0px; border-bottom-right-radius: 0px; border-bottom-left-radius: 0px;">Oppose Book Worship</em> (May 1930)</span><span class="suffix" style="display: none;"></span></h4>
<p data-tool="mdnice编辑器" style="color: rgb(74, 74, 74); font-size: 16px; line-height: 1.8em; letter-spacing: 0.02em; text-align: left; text-indent: 0em; margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; padding-top: 20px; padding-bottom: 8px; padding-left: 0px; padding-right: 0px;"><strong style="color: rgb(0, 0, 0); font-weight: bold; background-attachment: scroll; background-clip: border-box; background-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0); background-image: none; background-origin: padding-box; background-position-x: left; background-position-y: top; background-repeat: no-repeat; background-size: auto; width: auto; height: auto; margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; padding-top: 0px; padding-bottom: 0px; padding-left: 0px; padding-right: 0px; border-top-style: none; border-bottom-style: none; border-left-style: none; border-right-style: none; border-top-width: 3px; border-bottom-width: 3px; border-left-width: 3px; border-right-width: 3px; border-top-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.4); border-bottom-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.4); border-left-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.4); border-right-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.4); border-top-left-radius: 0px; border-top-right-radius: 0px; border-bottom-right-radius: 0px; border-bottom-left-radius: 0px;">Original Title</strong>: <em style="color: rgb(0, 0, 0); font-style: italic; background-attachment: scroll; background-clip: border-box; background-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0); background-image: none; background-origin: padding-box; background-position-x: left; background-position-y: top; background-repeat: no-repeat; background-size: auto; width: auto; height: auto; margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; padding-top: 0px; padding-bottom: 0px; padding-left: 0px; padding-right: 0px; border-top-style: none; border-bottom-style: none; border-left-style: none; border-right-style: none; border-top-width: 3px; border-bottom-width: 3px; border-left-width: 3px; border-right-width: 3px; border-top-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.4); border-bottom-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.4); border-left-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.4); border-right-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.4); border-top-left-radius: 0px; border-top-right-radius: 0px; border-bottom-right-radius: 0px; border-bottom-left-radius: 0px;">Investigation Work</em></p>
<p data-tool="mdnice编辑器" style="color: rgb(74, 74, 74); font-size: 16px; line-height: 1.8em; letter-spacing: 0.02em; text-align: left; text-indent: 0em; margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; padding-top: 20px; padding-bottom: 8px; padding-left: 0px; padding-right: 0px;"><strong style="color: rgb(0, 0, 0); font-weight: bold; background-attachment: scroll; background-clip: border-box; background-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0); background-image: none; background-origin: padding-box; background-position-x: left; background-position-y: top; background-repeat: no-repeat; background-size: auto; width: auto; height: auto; margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; padding-top: 0px; padding-bottom: 0px; padding-left: 0px; padding-right: 0px; border-top-style: none; border-bottom-style: none; border-left-style: none; border-right-style: none; border-top-width: 3px; border-bottom-width: 3px; border-left-width: 3px; border-right-width: 3px; border-top-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.4); border-bottom-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.4); border-left-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.4); border-right-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.4); border-top-left-radius: 0px; border-top-right-radius: 0px; border-bottom-right-radius: 0px; border-bottom-left-radius: 0px;">Core Golden Quotes</strong>:</p>
<blockquote class="custom-blockquote multiquote-1" data-tool="mdnice编辑器" style="margin-top: 20px; margin-bottom: 20px; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; padding-top: 10px; padding-bottom: 10px; padding-left: 20px; padding-right: 10px; border-top-style: none; border-bottom-style: none; border-left-style: none; border-right-style: none; border-top-width: 3px; border-bottom-width: 3px; border-left-width: 3px; border-right-width: 3px; border-top-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.4); border-bottom-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.4); border-left-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.4); border-right-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.4); border-top-left-radius: 0px; border-top-right-radius: 0px; border-bottom-right-radius: 0px; border-bottom-left-radius: 0px; background-attachment: scroll; background-clip: border-box; background-color: rgb(239, 239, 239); background-image: none; background-origin: padding-box; background-position-x: left; background-position-y: top; background-repeat: no-repeat; background-size: auto; width: auto; height: auto; box-shadow: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0) 0px 0px 0px 0px; display: block; overflow-x: auto; overflow-y: auto;"><span style="display: none; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); font-size: 16px; line-height: 1.5em; letter-spacing: 0em; text-align: left; font-weight: normal;"></span>
<p style="text-indent: 0em; padding-top: 20px; padding-bottom: 8px; padding-left: 0px; padding-right: 0px; color: rgb(89, 89, 89); font-size: 16px; line-height: 1.8em; letter-spacing: 0em; text-align: left; font-weight: normal; margin-top: 0px; margin-right: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; margin-left: 0px;">"No investigation, no right to speak."
"You can't solve that problem? Well, get down and investigate the present facts and its past history! When you have investigated the problem thoroughly, you will know how to solve it."</p>
</blockquote>
<p data-tool="mdnice编辑器" style="color: rgb(74, 74, 74); font-size: 16px; line-height: 1.8em; letter-spacing: 0.02em; text-align: left; text-indent: 0em; margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; padding-top: 20px; padding-bottom: 8px; padding-left: 0px; padding-right: 0px;"><strong style="color: rgb(0, 0, 0); font-weight: bold; background-attachment: scroll; background-clip: border-box; background-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0); background-image: none; background-origin: padding-box; background-position-x: left; background-position-y: top; background-repeat: no-repeat; background-size: auto; width: auto; height: auto; margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; padding-top: 0px; padding-bottom: 0px; padding-left: 0px; padding-right: 0px; border-top-style: none; border-bottom-style: none; border-left-style: none; border-right-style: none; border-top-width: 3px; border-bottom-width: 3px; border-left-width: 3px; border-right-width: 3px; border-top-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.4); border-bottom-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.4); border-left-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.4); border-right-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.4); border-top-left-radius: 0px; border-top-right-radius: 0px; border-bottom-right-radius: 0px; border-bottom-left-radius: 0px;">Why It Matters</strong>:
This article directly answers <em style="color: rgb(0, 0, 0); font-style: italic; background-attachment: scroll; background-clip: border-box; background-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0); background-image: none; background-origin: padding-box; background-position-x: left; background-position-y: top; background-repeat: no-repeat; background-size: auto; width: auto; height: auto; margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; padding-top: 0px; padding-bottom: 0px; padding-left: 0px; padding-right: 0px; border-top-style: none; border-bottom-style: none; border-left-style: none; border-right-style: none; border-top-width: 3px; border-bottom-width: 3px; border-left-width: 3px; border-right-width: 3px; border-top-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.4); border-bottom-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.4); border-left-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.4); border-right-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.4); border-top-left-radius: 0px; border-top-right-radius: 0px; border-bottom-right-radius: 0px; border-bottom-left-radius: 0px;">how</em> to achieve a "Clear Situation"—<strong style="color: rgb(0, 0, 0); font-weight: bold; background-attachment: scroll; background-clip: border-box; background-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0); background-image: none; background-origin: padding-box; background-position-x: left; background-position-y: top; background-repeat: no-repeat; background-size: auto; width: auto; height: auto; margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; padding-top: 0px; padding-bottom: 0px; padding-left: 0px; padding-right: 0px; border-top-style: none; border-bottom-style: none; border-left-style: none; border-right-style: none; border-top-width: 3px; border-bottom-width: 3px; border-left-width: 3px; border-right-width: 3px; border-top-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.4); border-bottom-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.4); border-left-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.4); border-right-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.4); border-top-left-radius: 0px; border-top-right-radius: 0px; border-bottom-right-radius: 0px; border-bottom-left-radius: 0px;">through investigation and research</strong>. Research and investigation must be done with a specific purpose and directed toward specific problems.</p>
<p data-tool="mdnice编辑器" style="color: rgb(74, 74, 74); font-size: 16px; line-height: 1.8em; letter-spacing: 0.02em; text-align: left; text-indent: 0em; margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; padding-top: 20px; padding-bottom: 8px; padding-left: 0px; padding-right: 0px;">In this text, Mao fiercely criticized dogmatists ("Book Worshipers") who did not understand China's actual reality and could only recite Marxist-Leninist classics. He proposed:</p>
<ul data-tool="mdnice编辑器" style="list-style-type: disc; margin-top: 8px; margin-bottom: 8px; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; padding-top: 0px; padding-bottom: 0px; padding-left: 25px; padding-right: 0px; color: rgb(0, 0, 0);">
<li><section style="margin-top: 5px; margin-bottom: 5px; color: rgb(1, 1, 1); font-size: 16px; line-height: 1.8em; letter-spacing: 0em; text-align: left; font-weight: normal;">Investigation is the foundation of all work.</section></li><li><section style="margin-top: 5px; margin-bottom: 5px; color: rgb(1, 1, 1); font-size: 16px; line-height: 1.8em; letter-spacing: 0em; text-align: left; font-weight: normal;">"The victory of the Chinese revolutionary struggle depends on the Chinese comrades' understanding of Chinese conditions."</section></li></ul>
<hr data-tool="mdnice编辑器" style="margin-top: 10px; margin-bottom: 10px; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; padding-top: 0px; padding-bottom: 0px; padding-left: 0px; padding-right: 0px; border-top-style: none; border-bottom-style: none; border-left-style: none; border-right-style: none; border-top-width: 1px; border-bottom-width: 3px; border-left-width: 3px; border-right-width: 3px; border-top-color: rgb(0, 0, 0); border-bottom-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.4); border-left-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.4); border-right-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.4); border-top-left-radius: 0px; border-top-right-radius: 0px; border-bottom-right-radius: 0px; border-bottom-left-radius: 0px; background-attachment: scroll; background-clip: border-box; background-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0); background-image: linear-gradient(90deg, rgba(60, 112, 198, 0) 0%, rgba(60, 122, 198, 0.75) 50%, rgba(60, 122, 198, 0) 100%); background-origin: padding-box; background-position-x: left; background-position-y: top; background-repeat: no-repeat; background-size: auto; width: auto; height: 1px;">
<h4 data-tool="mdnice编辑器" style="margin-top: 30px; margin-bottom: 15px; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; padding-top: 0px; padding-bottom: 0px; padding-left: 0px; padding-right: 0px; display: block;"><span class="prefix" style="display: none;"></span><span class="content" style="font-size: 18px; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 1.5em; letter-spacing: 0em; text-align: left; font-weight: bold; display: block;">The Second Most Important: <em style="color: rgb(0, 0, 0); font-style: italic; background-attachment: scroll; background-clip: border-box; background-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0); background-image: none; background-origin: padding-box; background-position-x: left; background-position-y: top; background-repeat: no-repeat; background-size: auto; width: auto; height: auto; margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; padding-top: 0px; padding-bottom: 0px; padding-left: 0px; padding-right: 0px; border-top-style: none; border-bottom-style: none; border-left-style: none; border-right-style: none; border-top-width: 3px; border-bottom-width: 3px; border-left-width: 3px; border-right-width: 3px; border-top-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.4); border-bottom-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.4); border-left-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.4); border-right-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.4); border-top-left-radius: 0px; border-top-right-radius: 0px; border-bottom-right-radius: 0px; border-bottom-left-radius: 0px;">On Practice</em> (July 1937)</span><span class="suffix" style="display: none;"></span></h4>
<p data-tool="mdnice编辑器" style="color: rgb(74, 74, 74); font-size: 16px; line-height: 1.8em; letter-spacing: 0.02em; text-align: left; text-indent: 0em; margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; padding-top: 20px; padding-bottom: 8px; padding-left: 0px; padding-right: 0px;"><strong style="color: rgb(0, 0, 0); font-weight: bold; background-attachment: scroll; background-clip: border-box; background-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0); background-image: none; background-origin: padding-box; background-position-x: left; background-position-y: top; background-repeat: no-repeat; background-size: auto; width: auto; height: auto; margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; padding-top: 0px; padding-bottom: 0px; padding-left: 0px; padding-right: 0px; border-top-style: none; border-bottom-style: none; border-left-style: none; border-right-style: none; border-top-width: 3px; border-bottom-width: 3px; border-left-width: 3px; border-right-width: 3px; border-top-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.4); border-bottom-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.4); border-left-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.4); border-right-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.4); border-top-left-radius: 0px; border-top-right-radius: 0px; border-bottom-right-radius: 0px; border-bottom-left-radius: 0px;">Subtitle</strong>: On the Relation Between Knowledge and Practice, Between Knowing and Doing</p>
<p data-tool="mdnice编辑器" style="color: rgb(74, 74, 74); font-size: 16px; line-height: 1.8em; letter-spacing: 0.02em; text-align: left; text-indent: 0em; margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; padding-top: 20px; padding-bottom: 8px; padding-left: 0px; padding-right: 0px;"><strong style="color: rgb(0, 0, 0); font-weight: bold; background-attachment: scroll; background-clip: border-box; background-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0); background-image: none; background-origin: padding-box; background-position-x: left; background-position-y: top; background-repeat: no-repeat; background-size: auto; width: auto; height: auto; margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; padding-top: 0px; padding-bottom: 0px; padding-left: 0px; padding-right: 0px; border-top-style: none; border-bottom-style: none; border-left-style: none; border-right-style: none; border-top-width: 3px; border-bottom-width: 3px; border-left-width: 3px; border-right-width: 3px; border-top-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.4); border-bottom-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.4); border-left-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.4); border-right-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.4); border-top-left-radius: 0px; border-top-right-radius: 0px; border-bottom-right-radius: 0px; border-bottom-left-radius: 0px;">Core Thought</strong>:</p>
<blockquote class="custom-blockquote multiquote-1" data-tool="mdnice编辑器" style="margin-top: 20px; margin-bottom: 20px; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; padding-top: 10px; padding-bottom: 10px; padding-left: 20px; padding-right: 10px; border-top-style: none; border-bottom-style: none; border-left-style: none; border-right-style: none; border-top-width: 3px; border-bottom-width: 3px; border-left-width: 3px; border-right-width: 3px; border-top-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.4); border-bottom-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.4); border-left-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.4); border-right-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.4); border-top-left-radius: 0px; border-top-right-radius: 0px; border-bottom-right-radius: 0px; border-bottom-left-radius: 0px; background-attachment: scroll; background-clip: border-box; background-color: rgb(239, 239, 239); background-image: none; background-origin: padding-box; background-position-x: left; background-position-y: top; background-repeat: no-repeat; background-size: auto; width: auto; height: auto; box-shadow: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0) 0px 0px 0px 0px; display: block; overflow-x: auto; overflow-y: auto;"><span style="display: none; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); font-size: 16px; line-height: 1.5em; letter-spacing: 0em; text-align: left; font-weight: normal;"></span>
<p style="text-indent: 0em; padding-top: 20px; padding-bottom: 8px; padding-left: 0px; padding-right: 0px; color: rgb(89, 89, 89); font-size: 16px; line-height: 1.8em; letter-spacing: 0em; text-align: left; font-weight: normal; margin-top: 0px; margin-right: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; margin-left: 0px;">"Practice, knowledge, again practice, and again knowledge. This form repeats itself in endless cycles, and with each cycle the content of practice and knowledge rises to a higher level."</p>
</blockquote>
<p data-tool="mdnice编辑器" style="color: rgb(74, 74, 74); font-size: 16px; line-height: 1.8em; letter-spacing: 0.02em; text-align: left; text-indent: 0em; margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; padding-top: 20px; padding-bottom: 8px; padding-left: 0px; padding-right: 0px;"><strong style="color: rgb(0, 0, 0); font-weight: bold; background-attachment: scroll; background-clip: border-box; background-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0); background-image: none; background-origin: padding-box; background-position-x: left; background-position-y: top; background-repeat: no-repeat; background-size: auto; width: auto; height: auto; margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; padding-top: 0px; padding-bottom: 0px; padding-left: 0px; padding-right: 0px; border-top-style: none; border-bottom-style: none; border-left-style: none; border-right-style: none; border-top-width: 3px; border-bottom-width: 3px; border-left-width: 3px; border-right-width: 3px; border-top-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.4); border-bottom-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.4); border-left-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.4); border-right-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.4); border-top-left-radius: 0px; border-top-right-radius: 0px; border-bottom-right-radius: 0px; border-bottom-left-radius: 0px;">Why It Matters</strong>:
This article discusses the epistemological basis of "Clear Situation" from a philosophical height:</p>
<ul data-tool="mdnice编辑器" style="list-style-type: disc; margin-top: 8px; margin-bottom: 8px; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; padding-top: 0px; padding-bottom: 0px; padding-left: 25px; padding-right: 0px; color: rgb(0, 0, 0);">
<li><section style="margin-top: 5px; margin-bottom: 5px; color: rgb(1, 1, 1); font-size: 16px; line-height: 1.8em; letter-spacing: 0em; text-align: left; font-weight: normal;">Knowledge comes from practice (not from sitting in a room thinking).</section></li><li><section style="margin-top: 5px; margin-bottom: 5px; color: rgb(1, 1, 1); font-size: 16px; line-height: 1.8em; letter-spacing: 0em; text-align: left; font-weight: normal;">Knowledge must be returned to practice for verification (no armchair strategies).</section></li><li><section style="margin-top: 5px; margin-bottom: 5px; color: rgb(1, 1, 1); font-size: 16px; line-height: 1.8em; letter-spacing: 0em; text-align: left; font-weight: normal;">It requires repeated cycles (the situation is dynamic, so investigation must be continuous).</section></li></ul>
<p data-tool="mdnice编辑器" style="color: rgb(74, 74, 74); font-size: 16px; line-height: 1.8em; letter-spacing: 0.02em; text-align: left; text-indent: 0em; margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; padding-top: 20px; padding-bottom: 8px; padding-left: 0px; padding-right: 0px;"><strong style="color: rgb(0, 0, 0); font-weight: bold; background-attachment: scroll; background-clip: border-box; background-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0); background-image: none; background-origin: padding-box; background-position-x: left; background-position-y: top; background-repeat: no-repeat; background-size: auto; width: auto; height: auto; margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; padding-top: 0px; padding-bottom: 0px; padding-left: 0px; padding-right: 0px; border-top-style: none; border-bottom-style: none; border-left-style: none; border-right-style: none; border-top-width: 3px; border-bottom-width: 3px; border-left-width: 3px; border-right-width: 3px; border-top-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.4); border-bottom-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.4); border-left-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.4); border-right-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.4); border-top-left-radius: 0px; border-top-right-radius: 0px; border-bottom-right-radius: 0px; border-bottom-left-radius: 0px;">Correspondence to the "Nine-Character Mantra"</strong>:</p>
<ul data-tool="mdnice编辑器" style="list-style-type: disc; margin-top: 8px; margin-bottom: 8px; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; padding-top: 0px; padding-bottom: 0px; padding-left: 25px; padding-right: 0px; color: rgb(0, 0, 0);">
<li><section style="margin-top: 5px; margin-bottom: 5px; color: rgb(1, 1, 1); font-size: 16px; line-height: 1.8em; letter-spacing: 0em; text-align: left; font-weight: normal;">Clear Situation = Obtaining correct knowledge through practice.</section></li><li><section style="margin-top: 5px; margin-bottom: 5px; color: rgb(1, 1, 1); font-size: 16px; line-height: 1.8em; letter-spacing: 0em; text-align: left; font-weight: normal;">Correct Method = Using correct knowledge to guide practice.</section></li></ul>
<hr data-tool="mdnice编辑器" style="margin-top: 10px; margin-bottom: 10px; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; padding-top: 0px; padding-bottom: 0px; padding-left: 0px; padding-right: 0px; border-top-style: none; border-bottom-style: none; border-left-style: none; border-right-style: none; border-top-width: 1px; border-bottom-width: 3px; border-left-width: 3px; border-right-width: 3px; border-top-color: rgb(0, 0, 0); border-bottom-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.4); border-left-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.4); border-right-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.4); border-top-left-radius: 0px; border-top-right-radius: 0px; border-bottom-right-radius: 0px; border-bottom-left-radius: 0px; background-attachment: scroll; background-clip: border-box; background-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0); background-image: linear-gradient(90deg, rgba(60, 112, 198, 0) 0%, rgba(60, 122, 198, 0.75) 50%, rgba(60, 122, 198, 0) 100%); background-origin: padding-box; background-position-x: left; background-position-y: top; background-repeat: no-repeat; background-size: auto; width: auto; height: 1px;">
<h4 data-tool="mdnice编辑器" style="margin-top: 30px; margin-bottom: 15px; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; padding-top: 0px; padding-bottom: 0px; padding-left: 0px; padding-right: 0px; display: block;"><span class="prefix" style="display: none;"></span><span class="content" style="font-size: 18px; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 1.5em; letter-spacing: 0em; text-align: left; font-weight: bold; display: block;">The Third Most Important: <em style="color: rgb(0, 0, 0); font-style: italic; background-attachment: scroll; background-clip: border-box; background-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0); background-image: none; background-origin: padding-box; background-position-x: left; background-position-y: top; background-repeat: no-repeat; background-size: auto; width: auto; height: auto; margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; padding-top: 0px; padding-bottom: 0px; padding-left: 0px; padding-right: 0px; border-top-style: none; border-bottom-style: none; border-left-style: none; border-right-style: none; border-top-width: 3px; border-bottom-width: 3px; border-left-width: 3px; border-right-width: 3px; border-top-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.4); border-bottom-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.4); border-left-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.4); border-right-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.4); border-top-left-radius: 0px; border-top-right-radius: 0px; border-bottom-right-radius: 0px; border-bottom-left-radius: 0px;">On Contradiction</em> (August 1937)</span><span class="suffix" style="display: none;"></span></h4>
<p data-tool="mdnice编辑器" style="color: rgb(74, 74, 74); font-size: 16px; line-height: 1.8em; letter-spacing: 0.02em; text-align: left; text-indent: 0em; margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; padding-top: 20px; padding-bottom: 8px; padding-left: 0px; padding-right: 0px;"><strong style="color: rgb(0, 0, 0); font-weight: bold; background-attachment: scroll; background-clip: border-box; background-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0); background-image: none; background-origin: padding-box; background-position-x: left; background-position-y: top; background-repeat: no-repeat; background-size: auto; width: auto; height: auto; margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; padding-top: 0px; padding-bottom: 0px; padding-left: 0px; padding-right: 0px; border-top-style: none; border-bottom-style: none; border-left-style: none; border-right-style: none; border-top-width: 3px; border-bottom-width: 3px; border-left-width: 3px; border-right-width: 3px; border-top-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.4); border-bottom-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.4); border-left-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.4); border-right-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.4); border-top-left-radius: 0px; border-top-right-radius: 0px; border-bottom-right-radius: 0px; border-bottom-left-radius: 0px;">Core Thought</strong>:</p>
<blockquote class="custom-blockquote multiquote-1" data-tool="mdnice编辑器" style="margin-top: 20px; margin-bottom: 20px; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; padding-top: 10px; padding-bottom: 10px; padding-left: 20px; padding-right: 10px; border-top-style: none; border-bottom-style: none; border-left-style: none; border-right-style: none; border-top-width: 3px; border-bottom-width: 3px; border-left-width: 3px; border-right-width: 3px; border-top-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.4); border-bottom-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.4); border-left-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.4); border-right-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.4); border-top-left-radius: 0px; border-top-right-radius: 0px; border-bottom-right-radius: 0px; border-bottom-left-radius: 0px; background-attachment: scroll; background-clip: border-box; background-color: rgb(239, 239, 239); background-image: none; background-origin: padding-box; background-position-x: left; background-position-y: top; background-repeat: no-repeat; background-size: auto; width: auto; height: auto; box-shadow: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0) 0px 0px 0px 0px; display: block; overflow-x: auto; overflow-y: auto;"><span style="display: none; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); font-size: 16px; line-height: 1.5em; letter-spacing: 0em; text-align: left; font-weight: normal;"></span>
<p style="text-indent: 0em; padding-top: 20px; padding-bottom: 8px; padding-left: 0px; padding-right: 0px; color: rgb(89, 89, 89); font-size: 16px; line-height: 1.8em; letter-spacing: 0em; text-align: left; font-weight: normal; margin-top: 0px; margin-right: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; margin-left: 0px;">"In studying a problem, we must shun subjectivity, one-sidedness and superficiality."
"Qualitatively different contradictions can only be resolved by qualitatively different methods."</p>
</blockquote>
<p data-tool="mdnice编辑器" style="color: rgb(74, 74, 74); font-size: 16px; line-height: 1.8em; letter-spacing: 0.02em; text-align: left; text-indent: 0em; margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; padding-top: 20px; padding-bottom: 8px; padding-left: 0px; padding-right: 0px;"><strong style="color: rgb(0, 0, 0); font-weight: bold; background-attachment: scroll; background-clip: border-box; background-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0); background-image: none; background-origin: padding-box; background-position-x: left; background-position-y: top; background-repeat: no-repeat; background-size: auto; width: auto; height: auto; margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; padding-top: 0px; padding-bottom: 0px; padding-left: 0px; padding-right: 0px; border-top-style: none; border-bottom-style: none; border-left-style: none; border-right-style: none; border-top-width: 3px; border-bottom-width: 3px; border-left-width: 3px; border-right-width: 3px; border-top-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.4); border-bottom-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.4); border-left-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.4); border-right-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.4); border-top-left-radius: 0px; border-top-right-radius: 0px; border-bottom-right-radius: 0px; border-bottom-left-radius: 0px;">Why It Matters</strong>:
This article teaches you "how to see the situation clearly":</p>
<ul data-tool="mdnice编辑器" style="list-style-type: disc; margin-top: 8px; margin-bottom: 8px; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; padding-top: 0px; padding-bottom: 0px; padding-left: 25px; padding-right: 0px; color: rgb(0, 0, 0);">
<li><section style="margin-top: 5px; margin-bottom: 5px; color: rgb(1, 1, 1); font-size: 16px; line-height: 1.8em; letter-spacing: 0em; text-align: left; font-weight: normal;">Distinguish between the principal contradiction and secondary contradictions.</section></li><li><section style="margin-top: 5px; margin-bottom: 5px; color: rgb(1, 1, 1); font-size: 16px; line-height: 1.8em; letter-spacing: 0em; text-align: left; font-weight: normal;">Distinguish between the principal aspect and the secondary aspect of a contradiction.</section></li><li><section style="margin-top: 5px; margin-bottom: 5px; color: rgb(1, 1, 1); font-size: 16px; line-height: 1.8em; letter-spacing: 0em; text-align: left; font-weight: normal;">Analyze concrete problems concretely (no "one size fits all").</section></li></ul>
<p data-tool="mdnice编辑器" style="color: rgb(74, 74, 74); font-size: 16px; line-height: 1.8em; letter-spacing: 0.02em; text-align: left; text-indent: 0em; margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; padding-top: 20px; padding-bottom: 8px; padding-left: 0px; padding-right: 0px;"><strong style="color: rgb(0, 0, 0); font-weight: bold; background-attachment: scroll; background-clip: border-box; background-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0); background-image: none; background-origin: padding-box; background-position-x: left; background-position-y: top; background-repeat: no-repeat; background-size: auto; width: auto; height: auto; margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; padding-top: 0px; padding-bottom: 0px; padding-left: 0px; padding-right: 0px; border-top-style: none; border-bottom-style: none; border-left-style: none; border-right-style: none; border-top-width: 3px; border-bottom-width: 3px; border-left-width: 3px; border-right-width: 3px; border-top-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.4); border-bottom-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.4); border-left-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.4); border-right-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.4); border-top-left-radius: 0px; border-top-right-radius: 0px; border-bottom-right-radius: 0px; border-bottom-left-radius: 0px;">The text cites "Song Jiang Attacking the Zhu Family Manor"</strong>:</p>
<blockquote class="custom-blockquote multiquote-1" data-tool="mdnice编辑器" style="margin-top: 20px; margin-bottom: 20px; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; padding-top: 10px; padding-bottom: 10px; padding-left: 20px; padding-right: 10px; border-top-style: none; border-bottom-style: none; border-left-style: none; border-right-style: none; border-top-width: 3px; border-bottom-width: 3px; border-left-width: 3px; border-right-width: 3px; border-top-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.4); border-bottom-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.4); border-left-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.4); border-right-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.4); border-top-left-radius: 0px; border-top-right-radius: 0px; border-bottom-right-radius: 0px; border-bottom-left-radius: 0px; background-attachment: scroll; background-clip: border-box; background-color: rgb(239, 239, 239); background-image: none; background-origin: padding-box; background-position-x: left; background-position-y: top; background-repeat: no-repeat; background-size: auto; width: auto; height: auto; box-shadow: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0) 0px 0px 0px 0px; display: block; overflow-x: auto; overflow-y: auto;"><span style="display: none; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); font-size: 16px; line-height: 1.5em; letter-spacing: 0em; text-align: left; font-weight: normal;"></span>
<p style="text-indent: 0em; padding-top: 20px; padding-bottom: 8px; padding-left: 0px; padding-right: 0px; color: rgb(89, 89, 89); font-size: 16px; line-height: 1.8em; letter-spacing: 0em; text-align: left; font-weight: normal; margin-top: 0px; margin-right: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; margin-left: 0px;">"In the novel <em style="color: rgb(0, 0, 0); font-style: italic; background-attachment: scroll; background-clip: border-box; background-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0); background-image: none; background-origin: padding-box; background-position-x: left; background-position-y: top; background-repeat: no-repeat; background-size: auto; width: auto; height: auto; margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; padding-top: 0px; padding-bottom: 0px; padding-left: 0px; padding-right: 0px; border-top-style: none; border-bottom-style: none; border-left-style: none; border-right-style: none; border-top-width: 3px; border-bottom-width: 3px; border-left-width: 3px; border-right-width: 3px; border-top-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.4); border-bottom-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.4); border-left-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.4); border-right-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.4); border-top-left-radius: 0px; border-top-right-radius: 0px; border-bottom-right-radius: 0px; border-bottom-left-radius: 0px;">Water Margin</em>, Song Jiang thrice attacked the Zhu Family Manor. Twice he was defeated because he was ignorant of the local conditions and used the wrong method. Later he changed his method; first he investigated the situation, and he familiarized himself with the maze of roads, then he broke up the alliance between the Li, Hu and Zhu Villages and sent his men in disguise into the enemy camp as a Trojan horse. And on the third occasion he won."</p>
</blockquote>
<p data-tool="mdnice编辑器" style="color: rgb(74, 74, 74); font-size: 16px; line-height: 1.8em; letter-spacing: 0.02em; text-align: left; text-indent: 0em; margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; padding-top: 20px; padding-bottom: 8px; padding-left: 0px; padding-right: 0px;"><strong style="color: rgb(0, 0, 0); font-weight: bold; background-attachment: scroll; background-clip: border-box; background-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0); background-image: none; background-origin: padding-box; background-position-x: left; background-position-y: top; background-repeat: no-repeat; background-size: auto; width: auto; height: auto; margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; padding-top: 0px; padding-bottom: 0px; padding-left: 0px; padding-right: 0px; border-top-style: none; border-bottom-style: none; border-left-style: none; border-right-style: none; border-top-width: 3px; border-bottom-width: 3px; border-left-width: 3px; border-right-width: 3px; border-top-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.4); border-bottom-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.4); border-left-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.4); border-right-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.4); border-top-left-radius: 0px; border-top-right-radius: 0px; border-bottom-right-radius: 0px; border-bottom-left-radius: 0px;"><em style="color: rgb(0, 0, 0); font-weight: bold; font-style: italic; background-attachment: scroll; background-clip: border-box; background-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0); background-image: none; background-origin: padding-box; background-position-x: left; background-position-y: top; background-repeat: no-repeat; background-size: auto; width: auto; height: auto; margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; padding-top: 0px; padding-bottom: 0px; padding-left: 0px; padding-right: 0px; border-top-style: none; border-bottom-style: none; border-left-style: none; border-right-style: none; border-top-width: 3px; border-bottom-width: 3px; border-left-width: 3px; border-right-width: 3px; border-top-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.4); border-bottom-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.4); border-left-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.4); border-right-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.4); border-top-left-radius: 0px; border-top-right-radius: 0px; border-bottom-right-radius: 0px; border-bottom-left-radius: 0px;">On Contradiction</em> explicitly states: "Ignorant of local conditions, used the wrong method" (Situation unclear, method incorrect)!</strong></p>
<hr data-tool="mdnice编辑器" style="margin-top: 10px; margin-bottom: 10px; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; padding-top: 0px; padding-bottom: 0px; padding-left: 0px; padding-right: 0px; border-top-style: none; border-bottom-style: none; border-left-style: none; border-right-style: none; border-top-width: 1px; border-bottom-width: 3px; border-left-width: 3px; border-right-width: 3px; border-top-color: rgb(0, 0, 0); border-bottom-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.4); border-left-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.4); border-right-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.4); border-top-left-radius: 0px; border-top-right-radius: 0px; border-bottom-right-radius: 0px; border-bottom-left-radius: 0px; background-attachment: scroll; background-clip: border-box; background-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0); background-image: linear-gradient(90deg, rgba(60, 112, 198, 0) 0%, rgba(60, 122, 198, 0.75) 50%, rgba(60, 122, 198, 0) 100%); background-origin: padding-box; background-position-x: left; background-position-y: top; background-repeat: no-repeat; background-size: auto; width: auto; height: 1px;">
<h3 data-tool="mdnice编辑器" style="margin-top: 30px; margin-bottom: 15px; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; padding-top: 0px; padding-bottom: 0px; padding-left: 0px; padding-right: 0px; align-items: unset; background-attachment: scroll; background-clip: border-box; background-color: transparent; background-image: none; background-origin: padding-box; background-position-x: 0%; background-position-y: 0%; background-repeat: no-repeat; background-size: auto; border-top-style: none; border-bottom-style: none; border-left-style: none; border-right-style: none; border-top-width: 1px; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-left-width: 1px; border-right-width: 1px; border-top-color: rgb(0, 0, 0); border-bottom-color: rgb(0, 0, 0); border-left-color: rgb(0, 0, 0); border-right-color: rgb(0, 0, 0); border-top-left-radius: 0px; border-top-right-radius: 0px; border-bottom-left-radius: 0px; border-bottom-right-radius: 0px; box-shadow: none; display: block; flex-direction: unset; float: unset; height: auto; justify-content: unset; line-height: 1.5em; overflow-x: unset; overflow-y: unset; position: relative; text-align: left; text-shadow: none; transform: none; width: auto; -webkit-box-reflect: unset;"><span style="background-attachment: scroll; background-clip: border-box; background-color: transparent; background-image: url('https://files.mdnice.com/mountain_1.png'); background-origin: padding-box; background-position-x: 0%; background-position-y: 0%; background-repeat: no-repeat; background-size: 15px 15px; width: 15px; height: 15px; align-items: unset; border-top-style: none; border-bottom-style: none; border-left-style: none; border-right-style: none; border-top-width: 1px; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-left-width: 1px; border-right-width: 1px; border-top-color: rgb(0, 0, 0); border-bottom-color: rgb(0, 0, 0); border-left-color: rgb(0, 0, 0); border-right-color: rgb(0, 0, 0); border-top-left-radius: 0px; border-top-right-radius: 0px; border-bottom-left-radius: 0px; border-bottom-right-radius: 0px; box-shadow: none; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); display: inline-block; font-size: 22px; font-weight: bold; flex-direction: unset; float: unset; justify-content: unset; letter-spacing: 0px; line-height: 1.5em; margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: -2px; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; overflow-x: unset; overflow-y: unset; padding-top: 0px; padding-bottom: 0px; padding-left: 0px; padding-right: 0px; position: relative; text-align: left; text-indent: 0em; text-shadow: none; transform: none; -webkit-box-reflect: unset;"></span><span class="prefix" style="display: none;"></span><span class="content" style="font-size: 16px; color: rgb(60, 112, 198); line-height: 1.5em; letter-spacing: 0em; align-items: unset; background-attachment: scroll; background-clip: border-box; background-color: transparent; background-image: none; background-origin: padding-box; background-position-x: 0%; background-position-y: 0%; background-repeat: no-repeat; background-size: auto; border-top-style: none; border-bottom-style: none; border-left-style: none; border-right-style: none; border-top-width: 1px; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-left-width: 1px; border-right-width: 1px; border-top-color: rgb(0, 0, 0); border-bottom-color: rgb(0, 0, 0); border-left-color: rgb(0, 0, 0); border-right-color: rgb(0, 0, 0); border-top-left-radius: 0px; border-top-right-radius: 0px; border-bottom-left-radius: 0px; border-bottom-right-radius: 0px; box-shadow: none; display: inline-block; font-weight: bold; flex-direction: unset; float: unset; height: auto; justify-content: unset; margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; margin-left: 8px; margin-right: 0px; overflow-x: unset; overflow-y: unset; padding-top: 0px; padding-bottom: 0px; padding-left: 0px; padding-right: 0px; position: relative; text-align: left; text-indent: 0em; text-shadow: none; transform: none; width: auto; -webkit-box-reflect: unset;">2. The Intellectual Source of [Great Resolve]</span><span class="suffix" style="display: none;"></span></h3>
<h4 data-tool="mdnice编辑器" style="margin-top: 30px; margin-bottom: 15px; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; padding-top: 0px; padding-bottom: 0px; padding-left: 0px; padding-right: 0px; display: block;"><span class="prefix" style="display: none;"></span><span class="content" style="font-size: 18px; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); line-height: 1.5em; letter-spacing: 0em; text-align: left; font-weight: bold; display: block;">The Most Core Article: <em style="color: rgb(0, 0, 0); font-style: italic; background-attachment: scroll; background-clip: border-box; background-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0); background-image: none; background-origin: padding-box; background-position-x: left; background-position-y: top; background-repeat: no-repeat; background-size: auto; width: auto; height: auto; margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; padding-top: 0px; padding-bottom: 0px; padding-left: 0px; padding-right: 0px; border-top-style: none; border-bottom-style: none; border-left-style: none; border-right-style: none; border-top-width: 3px; border-bottom-width: 3px; border-left-width: 3px; border-right-width: 3px; border-top-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.4); border-bottom-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.4); border-left-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.4); border-right-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.4); border-top-left-radius: 0px; border-top-right-radius: 0px; border-bottom-right-radius: 0px; border-bottom-left-radius: 0px;">On Protracted War</em> (May 1938)</span><span class="suffix" style="display: none;"></span></h4>
<p data-tool="mdnice编辑器" style="color: rgb(74, 74, 74); font-size: 16px; line-height: 1.8em; letter-spacing: 0.02em; text-align: left; text-indent: 0em; margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; padding-top: 20px; padding-bottom: 8px; padding-left: 0px; padding-right: 0px;"><strong style="color: rgb(0, 0, 0); font-weight: bold; background-attachment: scroll; background-clip: border-box; background-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0); background-image: none; background-origin: padding-box; background-position-x: left; background-position-y: top; background-repeat: no-repeat; background-size: auto; width: auto; height: auto; margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0px; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; padding-top: 0px; padding-bottom: 0px; padding-left: 0px; padding-right: 0px; border-top-style: none; border-bottom-style: none; border-left-style: none; border-right-style: none; border-top-width: 3px; border-bottom-width: 3px; border-left-width: 3px; border-right-width: 3px; border-top-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.4); border-bottom-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.4); border-left-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.4); border-right-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.4); border-top-left-radius: 0px; border-top-right-radius: 0px; border-bottom-right-radius: 0px; border-bottom-left-radius: 0px;">Background</strong>: In the early stages of the War of Resistance Against Japanese Aggression, two erroneous trends of thought existed domestically: "Theory of National Subjugation" and "Theory of Quick Victory."</p>
